Lightfoot 's heart sank .
Then he bound forward into that thicket .
He more than half expect to find no one there , but when he enter that thicket he receive the most wonderful surprise in all his life .
There stand Miss Daintyfoot , timid , bashful , but with a look in her eye which Lightfoot could not mistake .
In that instant Lightfoot understand the meaning of that longing which have keep him hunt for her and of the rage which have fill him when he have discover the presence of the big stranger from the Great Mountain .
It be love .
Lightfoot know that he love Miss Daintyfoot and , look into her soft , gentle eye , he know that Miss Daintyfoot love him .
CHAPTER XL HAPPY DAYS IN THE GREEN FOREST These be happy day in the Green Forest .
At least , they be happy for Lightfoot the Deer .
They be the happy day he have ever know .
You see , he have win beautiful , slender , young Miss Daintyfoot , and now she be no long Miss Daintyfoot but Mrs. Lightfoot .
Lightfoot be sure that there be no one anywhere so beautiful a she , and Mrs. Lightfoot know that there be no one so handsome and brave a he .
Wherever Lightfoot go , Mrs. Lightfoot go .
He show her all his favorite hiding-places .
He lead her to his favorite eating-places .
She do not tell him that she be already acquaint with every one of them , that she know the Green Forest quite as well a he do .
If he have stop to think how day after day she have manage to keep out of his sight while he hunt for her , he would have realize that there be little he could show her which she do not already know .
But he do n't stop to think and proudly lead her from place to place .
And Mrs. Lightfoot wisely express delight with all she saw quite a if it be all new .
Of course , all the little people of the Green Forest hurry to pay their respect to Mrs. Lightfoot and to tell Lightfoot how glad they felt for him .
And they really do feel glad .
You see , they all love Lightfoot and they know that now he would be happy than ever , and that there would be no danger of his leave the Green Forest because of loneliness .
The Green Forest would not be the same at all without Lightfoot the Deer .
Lightfoot tell Mrs. Lightfoot all about the terrible day of the hunting season and how glad he be that she have not be in the Green Forest then .
He tell her how the hunter with terrible gun have give him no rest and how he have have to swim the Big River to get away from the hound .
`` I know , '' reply Mrs. Lightfoot softly .
`` I know all about it .
You see , there be hunter on the Great Mountain .
In fact , that be how I happen to come down to the Green Forest .
They hunt me so up there that I do not dare stay , and I come down here think that there might be few hunter .
I would n't have believe that I could ever be thankful to hunter for anything , but I be , truly I be . ''
There be a puzzled look on Lightfoot 's face .
`` What for ? ''
he demand .
`` I ca n't imagine anybody be thankful to hunter for anything . ''
`` Oh , you stupid , '' cry Mrs. Lightfoot .
`` Do n't you see that if I have n't be drive down from the Great Mountain , I never would have find you ? ''
`` You mean , I never would have find you , '' retort Lightfoot .
`` I guess I owe these hunter more than you do .
I owe them the great happiness I have ever know , but I never would have think of it myself .
Is n't it queer how thing which seem the very bad possible sometimes turn out to be the very best possible ? ''
Blacky the Crow be one of Lightfoot 's friend , but sometimes even friend be envious .
It be so with Blacky .
He insist that he be quite as important in the Green Forest a be Lightfoot and that his doings be quite a interesting .

I THE LONE TRAVELER When Mistress Spring start from way down South to bring joy and gladness to the Green Meadows and the Green Forest , the Laughing Brook and the Smiling Pool , a great many traveler start with her or follow her .
Winsome Bluebird go just a little way ahead of her , for Winsome be the herald of Mistress Spring .
Then come Honker the Goose , and all the world hear his voice from way , way , up in the blue , blue sky know that truly Mistress Spring be on her way .
And with her come Little Friend the Song Sparrow , and Cheerful Robin and Mr. and Mrs. Redwing .
Then follow other traveler , ever so many of them , all eager to get back to the beautiful Green Forest and Green Meadows .
Now there be a few feathered folk who think the far away South be quite good enough for them to live there all the year round .
Ol ' Mistah Buzzard use to think that way .
Indeed , he use to think that there be no place like the dear `` Ol ' Souf , '' and it be n't until he go look for his old friend , Unc ' Billy Possum , who have come up to live in the Green Forest , that he find out how nice it be where the Laughing Brook dance down through the Green Forest to the Smiling Pool and then through the Green Meadows to the Big River .

Of course Ol ' Mistah Buzzard have wonderful story to tell when he go back South in the fall , and all winter long he warm his toe on the chimney top while he tell his friend about the wonderful thing he have see in his travel .
Now there be a certain friend of his , and of Unc ' Billy Possum , who have listen to these story for a long time without seem in the least interested .

But he do n't say a word , not a word .

He do n't say anything about it to any one , but he just start off by himself .
Now of course he do n't know the way , never have be that way before , but he keep on go and go , keep out of sight as much a he could , and ask no question .

`` All Ah do get to do be to keep on go till Ah see Brer Buzzard , '' think he .
So he travel and travel without speak to any one , and always look up in the blue , blue sky .
Then one day he saw a black speck high up in the blue , blue sky , and it go round and round and round and round .
Finally it drop down , down , down until it disappear among the tree .
`` It 's Brer Buzzard and that must be the Green Forest where Unc ' Billy Possum live , '' think the lone traveler , and chuckle .
`` Ah reckon Ah 'll give Unc ' Billy a surprise .
Yes , Sah , Ah reckon so . ''
And all the time Unc ' Billy Possum and Ol ' Mistah Buzzard know nothing at all about the come of their old friend and neighbor , but think him far , far away down in Ol ' Virginny where they have leave him .

V SAMMY JAY IS INDIGNANT Sammy Jay be indignant .

Now he know that he could go to sleep in peace , just a he always have .

He have be so worried lately that he have n't take much care of himself , which be very unusual for Sammy Jay .
Now , however , he felt so much good that he begin to think about his look .
When he have finish dressing , he start for the alder beside the Laughing Brook just to have a look around .
Of course he do n't expect to find his voice down there , for who ever saw a voice ?
Still he think that he might find something that would explain the mystery .
He hunt all around in the thicket of alder beside the Laughing Brook , but nothing unusual do he find .
Then for a long time he sit as still a still can be , study and thinking .
Finally he think to himself : `` I 'll just see how my voice really do sound down here , '' and open his mouth he scream : `` Thief !
thief !
thief ! ''
Then out pop Jenny Wren , and she be so mad that she could n't sit still a second .
My , my , my , how she do scold !
`` You ought to be ashamed of yourself , Sammy Jay !
You ought to be ashamed of yourself ! ''
she sputter .
`` Is n't it enough to keep u awake half the night without come down and scream all day ? ''
`` I have n't be down here in the night , and I have n't keep anybody awake ! ''
reply Sammy Jay indignantly .
Jenny Wren come right up in front of Sammy Jay and hop up and down .
She be so mad that with every word she jerk her funny little tail so that Sammy Jay almost have to laugh .
`` Do n't tell that to me , Sammy Jay !
Do n't tell that to me ! ''
she cry .
`` Did n't I see you with my own eye sit in that alder over there ?
Do n't tell that to me !
You ought to be ashamed of yourself ! ''
X SAMMY JAY SEEKS ADVICE Sammy Jay have a headache , such a headache !
He have think and think and think , until now it seem to him that the world surely have turn topsy-turvy .
His poor little head be all in a whirl , and that be what make it ache .
First he have be accuse of scream in the night to waken and scare the little meadow and forest people who want to sleep .
Then he have keep awake all night to find out what it mean , and he have hear what sound like his own voice scream `` Thief !
thief !
thief ! ''
down by the Laughing Brook , when all the time he be sit in the dark in his own big pine-tree in the Green Forest .
That be bad enough , but to have Jenny Wren tell him that she have see him with her own eye sit in an alder tree and screaming , at the very time that he have be back there in the big pine-tree , be more than Sammy Jay could stand .
It be no wonder that his head ache .
Hardly any of the little meadow and forest people would speak to him now .
They just turn their back to him whenever he meet them .
He do n't mind this so much , because he know that none of them have ever like him very well .
You see he have play too many mean trick for any one to really like him .
But he do hate to have them blame him for something that he have n't do .
`` It 's too much for me ! ''
say Sammy Jay .
`` It 's too much for me !
I 've think and think , until my brain just go round and round and make me dizzy , and my thought turn somersault over each other .
I must get help somewhere .
Now , who can I go to , so few will have anything to do with me ? ''
`` Caw , caw , caw ! ''
Sammy Jay prick up his ear and spread his wing .
`` My cousin , Blacky the Crow ! ''
he cry .
`` Why do n't I think of him before ?
He 's very smart , be Blacky the Crow , and perhaps he can tell me what to do . ''
So Sammy Jay hurry a fast a he could to lay his trouble before Blacky the Crow .
Blacky 's eye twinkle a he listen to Sammy Jay 's tale of woe .
When Sammy have finish and have ask for Blacky 's advice , Blacky go into a black study .
Sammy sit and wait patiently , for he felt certain that Blacky 's shrewd head would find some plan to solve the mystery .
`` I do n't know how you can find out who it be that 's make you all this trouble , but I 'll tell you how you can prove that it be n't you that scream in the night , '' say Blacky the Crow after a while .
`` How ? ''
ask Sammy Jay eagerly .
`` Go away from the Green Meadows and the Green Forest and stay away for a week , '' reply Blacky the Crow .
`` Go up to the far-away Old Pasture on the edge of the mountain , where Reddy and Granny Fox be live .
Have Boomer the Nighthawk see you go to bed there , and then ask him to come straight down here and tell Peter Rabbit just where you be .
Peter will tell every one else , for he ca n't keep his tongue still , and then they 'll all know that it be n't you that scream in the night . ''
`` The very thing ! ''
cry Sammy Jay .
`` I 'll move at once ! ''
And off he hurry to prepare to move up to the Old Pasture .
XI HOW BLACKY THE CROW 'S PLAN WORKED OUT `` Thief !
thief !
thief ! ''
Old Granny Fox , trot along a cow-path in the Old Pasture on the edge of the mountain , hear it and grin .
Reddy Fox , sit in the doorway of their new home under the great rock in the midst of the thick clump of bush and young tree , hear it , too , and he grin even more broadly than Granny Fox .
It sound good to him , do that harsh scream , for it be the first time he have hear the voice of a single one of the little meadow and forest people since he and Granny Fox have move up to the lonesome Old Pasture .
`` Now I wonder what have bring Sammy Jay way up here ? ''

He tell how he have sit up all night and have hear what sound like his own voice , when all the time he be sit with his mouth shut as tight a tight could be .

Sammy scream twice .

He find Peter and tell him .
Of course Peter be very much surprise and , because he can not keep his tongue still , he start off at once to tell everybody he could find , just a Blacky the Crow have think he would do .
XII NO ONE BELIEVES PETER RABBIT Peter Rabbit sit in his secret place in the middle of the Old Briar-patch .

This be great news , and Peter could hardly wait for Boomer to stop talk , he be so anxious to spread the news over the Green Meadows and through the Green Forest , for Peter be a great gossip and can not keep his tongue still .

But no one believe him .
`` Wait and see !
Wait and see ! ''

`` Perhaps he do and then again perhaps he do n't , '' reply Bobby Coon , carefully wash an ear of sweet milky corn that he have bring down to the Laughing Brook from Farmer Brown 's corn-field , for Bobby Coon be very , very neat and always wash his food before eating .

thief !
thief ! ''
over in the alder bush .

So now Peter sit in the Old Briar-patch thinking and thinking , when he should have be asleep .

XIII STICKY-TOES THE TREE TOAD POURS OUT HIS TROUBLES Sticky-toes be quite upset .

XIV PETER RABBIT MEETS UNC ' BILLY POSSUM After Sticky-toes the Tree Toad have pour out his trouble , Peter go back to the Old Briar-patch , more puzzled than ever .

XV PETER RABBIT AND UNC ' BILLY POSSUM KEEP WATCH `` Now , '' say Peter Rabbit , a they settle themselves to watch , `` we 'll see for ourselves whether Sammy Jay and Sticky-toes have be tell the truth , or if they have be dream .

whisper Sticky-toes .

thief !
thief ! ''
from the very spot where they have just hear the voice of Sticky-toes .

XVI UNC ' BILLY POSSUM DOES A LITTLE SURPRISING HIMSELF When Unc ' Billy Possum first hear what sound like the voice of Sticky-toes the Tree Toad , he have think , just a Peter Rabbit do , that Sticky-toes be over in an alder tree on the other side of the Laughing Brook .

thief !
thief ! ''

XVII THE MEETING OF TWO OLD FRIENDS `` Why , Unc ' Billy Possum !

Yes , Sah , Ah reckon so .

The owner of the long tail and sharp eye throw back his head and laugh , and his laugh be like the most beautiful music .

thief ! ''

XVIII THE MISCHIEF-MAKERS There be a dreadful time on the Green Meadows and in the Green Forest .
Oh , dear , dear , dear !
It really be dreadful !
First Sammy Jay have be accuse of scream in the night and keep honest little meadow and forest people awake when they want to sleep .
And all the time Sammy Jay have n't make a sound .
Then Sticky-toes the Tree Toad have be accuse of be noisy , when all the time he be sit with his mouth close as tight a tight could be .
All this be bad enough , but now thing be so much bad that it be get so that no one would have anything to do with any one else .
Those who have be the very best of friend would pass without speaking .
You see , everybody on the Green Meadows and in the Green Forest know everybody else by their voice .
So when Jimmy Skunk , happen along near the Smiling Pool , hear Mrs. Redwing 's voice , he do n't waste any time try to see Mrs. Redwing .
Instead , he go straight over and tell Johnny Chuck the unkind thing that he have overheard Mrs. Redwing say about Johnny .
In the same way Bobby Coon hear the voice of Blacky the Crow in Farmer Brown 's corn-field , and when Bobby listen , he hear some thing not at all nice about himself .
And so it be , all over the Green Meadows and through the Green Forest .
It seem a if almost everybody be hear talk about some one else , and never say nice thing .
The only one who still manage to keep on good term with everybody be Unc ' Billy Possum .
No one have ever hear him say unkind thing about others and so , because now there be so few others to talk to , everybody be glad to see Unc ' Billy come , and he soon be the best liked of all the little meadow and forest people .
He go about try to smooth out the trouble , and to see him you never , never would have guess that he have anything to do with make them .
My , my , no , indeed !
But every night when the moon be up , Unc ' Billy would have a caller , who would come and sit just outside the doorway of Unc ' Billy 's house and scream `` Thief !
thief !
thief ! ''
Then out would pop Unc ' Billy 's sharp little face , and then his fat little body would follow , and he and his friend with the long tail and the sharp eye , for of course you have guess that be who it be , would put their head together and laugh and chuckle a if they be enjoy the best joke ever be .
Then they would whisper and sometimes talk right out loud , when they felt sure that no one be near to hear .
What be they talk about ?
Why , about the trouble on the Green Meadows and in the Green Forest , and what a joke it all be , and what be the best way to keep it up .
You see , the reason that no one heard Unc ' Billy say mean thing or hear any mean thing say about Unc ' Billy be because it be Unc ' Billy himself and his friend with the long tail and the sharp eye who be make all the trouble .
Yes , Sir , they be the mischief-maker .
It be great fun to fool everybody so .
They never once stop to think how very , very uncomfortable it keep everybody feeling .
XIX BOBBY COON MAKES A DISCOVERY Bobby Coon have oversleep .
Usually Bobby be astir shortly after jolly , round , red Mr. Sun have go to bed behind the Purple Hills .
But Bobby be very irregular in his habit .
He be very fond of travel about in the night , be Bobby Coon , and when he do that , he sleep the great part of the day .
But once in a while he take a notion to travel about by daylight , and when he do that , why of course he have to sleep part of the night , anyway .
Bobby Coon be a very lucky chap , very lucky indeed , for he can see in the dark , and yet , unlike Hooty the Owl , he have no trouble in see in the broad daylight as well .
This night Bobby Coon have oversleep because he have not go to bed until the middle of the day .
He have be prowl about and get into mischief all of the night before and have not start for home until jolly , round Mr. Sun be smile down from right overhead .
By this time Bobby Coon have stick in his eye .
He be so sleepy that it seem to him that he never , never could get home .
He be stumble along through the Green Forest when he come to a hollow log .
What do you think he do ?
Why , he crawl in there , and in two minute be fast asleep , just as comfortable a if he have be in his own hollow tree .
There Bobby sleep all the rest of the day and until long after Mr. Sun have pull on his rosy nightcap .
Perhaps he would have sleep there all night , if he have n't be wake up .
It be the cry of `` Thief !
thief !
thief ! ''
that wake him .
It seem to come from right over his head .
`` Sammy Jay ought to be ashamed of himself , wake honest people like this ! ''
mutter Bobby Coon , a he yawn and stretch .
At first he could n't think where he be .
Then he remember .
He be just get ready to crawl out of the hollow log , when he hear something which make him stop and try to sit up so suddenly that he bump his head .
What he hear be the voice of Unc ' Billy Possum , and he know by the sound that Unc ' Billy be sit on the very log in which he himself be hide .
`` This be the great joke that ever be ! ''
say Unc ' Billy .
`` Pretty soon nobody on the Green Meadows or in the Green Forest will speak to anybody else except me .
Yo ' cert ` nly have get all your ol ' trick with yo ' . ''
`` Yes , '' reply a voice which Bobby Coon have never hear before , but which he know right away must belong to some one who have come from way down South where Unc ' Billy Possum and Ol ' Mistah Buzzard have come from .
`` Yes , '' say the voice , `` Ah do get all mah ol ' trick and some more .
But it 's easy , Unc ' Billy , it 's easy to fool your new friend , because Ah reckon they never have be fool this way before .
Don ' yo ' think it be most time to stop ?
Ah do n't want to show mahself in daylight .
Besides , if Ah 'm find out , nobody ai n't gwine to have anything to do with me . ''
`` Do n't yo ' worry .
Nobody 's gwine to find yo ' out .
We 'll keep it up just a day or two long .
Yo ' cert ` nly be powerful good at imitate other people 's voice .
Ah wonder that Ol ' Mistah Buzzard have n't get his eye on yo ' before now , '' say Unc ' Billy Possum .
Bobby Coon have become wide awake a he listen .
He try hard to get a peep at the stranger with Unc ' Billy , but all he could see be a long tail of feather .
Bobby wait until Unc ' Billy and his friend have leave .
Then he crawl out of the hollow log , and he be chuckle to himself .
`` I 'll just have a little talk with Ol ' Mistah Buzzard , '' say Bobby to himself .
XX BOBBY COON AND OL ' MISTAH BUZZARD HAVE A TALK Bobby Coon have spend the large part of the forenoon sit at the foot of the tall dead tree on which Ol ' Mistah Buzzard like to roost .
All the time Ol ' Mistah Buzzard have be sail ` round and ` round in circle way up in the blue , blue sky , sometimes so high that to Bobby he look like just a tiny speck .
Bobby have watch him until his own neck ache .
Mistah Buzzard hardly ever move his wing .
He just sail and sail and sail up and down and ` round and ` round , just a if it be no work at all but pure fun , a indeed it be .
Bobby Coon have wait so long that it be almost more than he could do to be patient any longer , but if you really want a thing , it be worth wait for , and so Bobby give a great sigh and try to make himself more comfortable .
At last Mistah Buzzard come sail down straight for the tall dead tree .

`` Fair to middle well , '' say Ol ' Mistah Buzzard , with a twinkle in his eye .

`` If you please , Mistah Buzzard , you can tell me if there be anybody way down South where you come from who can make his voice sound just like the voice of other people .
Is there ? ''
Bobby be use his very polite manner .
`` Cert ` nly !
Cert ` nly ! ''
chuckle Ol ' Mistah Buzzard .
`` It 's Mistah Mockah the Mocking-bird .

XXVI MR. MOCKER MAKES HIMSELF AT HOME At first , when the little meadow and forest people be ask to pardon the trick that Mr. Mocker and Unc ' Billy Possum have play , a few be incline not to .

Ol ' Mistah Buzzard laugh when he hear that some folk say that Mr. Mocker have not come by his voice honestly .
`` There be n't a word of truth in it , Brer Rabbit , '' he declare .
`` Yo ' go tell all your friend that Mistah Mockah be the best loved of all the bird way down Souf . ''
And this be all for the present about the adventure of Mr. Mocker the Mocking-bird .
But others have have adventure , and one be Jerry Muskrat .
The next book will tell all about them .

CHAPTER I Paddy the Beaver Begins Work .
Work , work all the night While the star be shin bright ; Work , work all the day ; I have get no time to play .
This little rhyme Paddy the Beaver make up a he toil at build the dam which be to make the pond he so much desired deep in the Green Forest .
Of course it be n't quite true , that about work all night and all day .
Nobody could do that , you know , and keep it up .
Everybody have to rest and sleep .
Yes , and everybody have to play a little to be at their best .
So it be n't quite true that Paddy work all day after work all night .
But it be true that Paddy have no time to play .
He have too much to do .
He have have his playtime during the long summer , and now he have to get ready for the long , cold winter .
Now , of all the little worker in the Green Forest , on the Green Meadows , and in the Smiling Pool , none can compare with Paddy the Beaver , not even his cousin , Jerry Muskrat .
Happy Jack Squirrel and Striped Chipmunk store up food for the long , cold month when rough Brother North Wind and Jack Frost rule , and Jerry Muskrat build a fine house wherein to keep warm and comfortable , but all this be as nothing to the work of Paddy the Beaver .
As I say before , Paddy have have a long playtime through the summer .
He have wander up and down the Laughing Brook .
He have follow it way up to the place where it start .
And all the time he have be study and study to make sure that he want to stay in the Green Forest .
In the first place , he have to be sure that there be plenty of the kind of food that he like .
Then he have to be equally sure that he could make a pond near where this particular food grow .
Last of all , he have to satisfy himself that if he do make a pond and build a home , he would be reasonably safe in it .
And all these thing he have do in his playtime .
Now he be ready to go to work , and when Paddy begin work , he stick to it until it be finish .
He say that be the only way to succeed , and you know and I know that he be right .
Now Paddy the Beaver can see at night just a Reddy Fox and Peter Rabbit and Bobby Coon can , and he like the night best , because he feel safe then .
But he can see in the daytime too , and when he feel that he be perfectly safe and no one be watch , he work then too .
Of course , the first thing to do be to build a dam across the Laughing Brook to make the pond he so much need .
He choose a low , open place deep in the Green Forest , around the edge of which grow many young aspen tree , the bark of which be his favorite food .
Through the middle of this open place flow the Laughing Brook .
At the low edge be just the place for a dam .
It would not have to be very long , and when it be finish and the water be stop in the Laughing Brook , it would just have to flow over the low , open place and make a pond there .
Paddy 's eye twinkle when he first saw it .
It be right then that he make up his mind to stay in the Green Forest .
So now that he be ready to begin his dam he go up the Laughing Brook to a place where alder and willow grow , and there he begin work ; that work be the cutting of a great number of tree by mean of his big front teeth which be give him for just this purpose .
And a he work , Paddy be happy , for one can never be truly happy who do no work .
CHAPTER II Paddy Plans a Pond .
Paddy the Beaver be busy cut down tree for the dam he have plan to build .
Up in the wood of the North from which he have come to the Green Forest , he have learn all about tree-cutting and dam-building and canal-digging and house-building .
Paddy 's father and mother have be very wise in the Beaver world , and Paddy have be quick to learn .
So now he know just what to do and the best way of do it .
You know , a great many people waste time and labor do thing the wrong way , so that they have to be do over again .
They forget to be sure they be right , and so they go ahead until they find they be wrong , and all their work go for nothing .
But Paddy the Beaver be n't this kind .
Paddy would never have leap into the spring with the steep side without look , a Grandfather Frog do .
So now he carefully pick out the tree to cut .
He could not afford to waste time cut down a tree that be n't go to be just what he want when it be down .
When he be sure that the tree be right , he look up at the top to find out whether , when he have cut it , it would fall clear of other tree .
He have learn to do that when he be quite young and heedless .

You know Paddy have the most wonderful teeth for cut .

He would begin by make a deep bite , and then another just a little way below .
Then he would pry out the little piece of wood between .

This be easy work , for he could take off a good-sized branch with one bite .

CHAPTER IX Paddy Plans a House .

With that Paddy slip into the water and swim all around his new pond to make sure of just the best place to build his house .
Now , place one 's house in just the right place be a very important matter .
Some people be dreadfully careless about this .
Jimmy Skunk , for instance , often make the mistake of dig his house -LRB- you know Jimmy make his house underground -RRB- right where everyone who happen along that way will see it .
Perhaps that be because Jimmy be so independent that he do n't care who know where he live .
But Paddy the Beaver never be careless .
He always choose just the very best place .
He make sure that it be best before he begin .
So now , although he be quite positive just where his house should be , he swim around the pond to make doubly sure .
Then , when he be quite satisfied , he swim over to the place he have choose .
It be where the water be quite deep .
`` There must n't be the least chance that the ice will ever get thick enough too close up my doorway , say he , `` and I 'm sure it never will here .
I must make the foundation strong and the wall thick .
I must have plenty of mud to plaster with , and inside , up above the water , I must have the snug , warm room where I can sleep in comfort .
This be the place to build it , and it be high time I be at work . ''
With that Paddy swam over to the place where he have cut the tree for his dam , and his heart be light , for he have long ago learn that the sure way to be happy be to be busy .
CHAPTER X Paddy Starts His House .
Jerry Muskrat be very much interested when he find that Paddy the Beaver , who you know , be his cousin , be build a house .
Jerry be a house-builder himself , and down deep in his heart he very much doubt if Paddy could build a good a house a he could .
His house be down in the Smiling Pool , and Jerry think it a very wonderful house indeed , and be very proud of it .
It be build of mud and sod and little alder and willow twig and bulrush .
Jerry have spend one winter in it , and he have decide to spend another there after he have fix it up a little .
So , as long a he do n't have to build a brand-new house , he could afford the time to watch his cousin Paddy .
Perhaps he hop that Paddy would ask his advice .
But Paddy do nothing of the kind .
He have see Jerry Muskrat 's house , and he have smile .
But he have take great pain not to let Jerry see that smile .
He would n't have hurt Jerry 's feeling for the world .
He be too polite and good-natured to do anything like that .
So Jerry sit on the end of an old log and watch Paddy work .
The first thing to build be the foundation .
This be of mud and grass with stick work into it to hold it together .
Paddy dig the mud from the bottom of his new pond .
And because the pond be new , there be a great deal of grassy sod there , which be just what Paddy need .
It be very convenient .
Jerry watch a little while and then , because Jerry be a worker himself , he just have to get busy and help .
Rather timidly he tell his big cousin that he would like to have a share in build the new house .
`` All right , '' reply Paddy , `` that will be fine .
You can bring mud while I be get the stick and grass . ''
So Jerry dive down to the bottom of the pond and dig up mud and pile it on the foundation and be happy .
The little star look down and twinkled merrily a they watch the two worker .
So the foundation grow and grow down under the water .
Jerry be very much surprise at the size of it .
It be ever and ever so much big than the foundation for his own house .
You see , he have forget how much big Paddy be .
Each night Jerry and Paddy work , rest during the daytime .
Occasionally Bobby Coon or Reddy Fox or Unc ' Billy Possum or Jimmy Skunk would come to the edge of the pond to see what be go on .
Peter Rabbit come every night .
But they could n't see much because , you know , Paddy and Jerry be work under water .
But at last Peter be reward .
There , just above the water , be a splendid platform of mud and grass and stick .
A great many stick be carefully lay as soon a the platform be above the water , for Paddy be very particular about this .
You see , it be to be the floor for the splendid room he be plan to build .
When it suit him , he begin to pile mud in the very middle .
Jerry puzzle and puzzle over this .
Where be Paddy 's room go to be , if he pile up the mud that way ?
But he do n't like to ask question , so he keep right on help .
Paddy would dive down to the bottom and then come up with double handful of mud , which he hold against his chest .
He would scramble out onto the platform and waddle over to the pile in the middle , where he would put the mud and pat it down .
Then back to the bottom for more .
And so the mud pile grow and grow , until it be quite two foot high .
`` Now , '' say Paddy , `` I 'll build the wall , and I guess you ca n't help me much with those .
I 'm go to begin them tomorrow night .
Perhaps you will like to see me do it , Cousin Jerry . ''
`` I certainly will , '' reply Jerry , still puzzle over that pile of mud in the middle .
CHAPTER XI Peter Rabbit and Jerry Muskrat Are Puzzled .
Jerry Muskrat be more and more sure that his big cousin , Paddy the Beaver , do n't know quite so much a he might about house-building .
Jerry would have like to offer some suggestion , but he do n't quite dare .
You see , he be very anxious not to displease his big cousin .
But he felt that he simply have get to speak his mind to someone , so he swim across to where he have see Peter Rabbit almost every night since Paddy begin to build .
Sure enough , Peter be there , sit up very straight and star with big round eye at the platform of mud and stick out in the water where Paddy the Beaver be at work .
`` Well , Peter , what do you think of it ? ''
ask Jerry `` What be it ? ''
ask Peter innocently .
`` Is it another dam ? ''
Jerry throw back his head and laugh and laugh .
Peter look at him suspiciously .
`` I do n't see anything to laugh at , '' say he .
`` Why , it 's a house , you stupid .
It 's Paddy 's new house , '' reply Jerry , wipe the tear of laughter from his eye .
`` I 'm not stupid ! ''
retort Peter .
`` How be I to know that that pile of mud and stick be mean for a house ?
It certainly do n't look it .
Where be the door ? ''
`` To tell you the truth , I do n't think it be much of a house myself , '' reply Jerry .
`` It have get a door , all right .
In fact it have get three .
You ca n't see them because they be under water , and there be a passage from each right up through that platform of mud and stick , which be the foundation of the house .
It really be a very fine foundation , Peter ; it really be .
But what I ca n't understand be what Paddy be think of by building that great pile of mud right in the middle .
When he get his wall build , where will his bedroom be ?
There wo n't be any room at all .
It wo n't be a house at all -- just a big useless pile of stick and mud .
Peter scratch his head and then pull his whisker thoughtfully a he gaze out at the pile in the water where Paddy the Beaver be at work .
`` It do look foolish , that 's a fact , '' say he .
`` Why do n't you point out to him the mistake he be make , Jerry ?
You have build such a splendid house yourself that you ought to be able to help Paddy and show him his mistake . ''
Jerry have smile a very self-satisfied smile when Peter mention his fine house , but he shake his head at the suggestion that he should give Paddy advice .
`` I -- I do n't just like to , '' he confess .
`` You know , he might not like it and -- and it do n't seem a if it would be quite polite .
Peter sniffed .
`` That would n't trouble me any if he be my cousin , '' say he .
Jerry shake his head , `` No , I do n't believe it would , '' he reply , `` but it do trouble me and -- and -- well , I think I 'll wait awhile . ''
Now all this time Paddy have be hard at work .
He be bring the long branch which he have cut from the tree out of which he have build his dam , and a lot of slender willow and alder pole .
He push these ahead of him a he swim .
When he reach the foundation of his house , he would lean them against the pile of mud in the middle with their big end rest on the foundation .
So he work all the way around until by and by the mud pile in the middle could n't be see .
It be completely cover with stick , and they be cunningly fasten together at the top .
CHAPTER XII Jerry Muskrat Learns Something If you think you know it all You be rid for a fall .
Use your ear and use your eye , But hold your tongue and you 'll be wise .
Jerry Muskrat will tell you that be as true a true can be .
Jerry know .
He find it out for himself .
Now he be very careful what he say about other people or what they be do .
But he be n't so careful when his cousin , Paddy the Beaver , be build his house .
No , Sir , Jerry be n't so careful then .
He though he know more about build a house than Paddy do .
He be sure of it when he watch Paddy heap up a great pile of mud right in the middle where his room ought to be , and then build a wall of stick around it .
He say as much to Peter Rabbit .
Now it be never safe to say anything to Peter Rabbit that you do n't care to have others know .
Peter have a great deal of respect for Jerry Muskrat 's opinion on house-building .
You see , he very much admires Jerry 's snug house in the Smiling Pool .
It really be a very fine house , and Jerry may be excuse for be proud of it .
But that do n't excuse Jerry for think that he know all there be to know about house-building .
Of course Peter tell everyone he meet that Paddy the Beaver be make a foolish mistake in build his house , and that Jerry Muskrat , who ought to know , say so .
So whenever they get the chance , the little people of the Green Forest and Green Meadows would steal up to the shore of Paddy 's new pond and chuckle a they look out at the great pile of stick and mud which Paddy have build for a house , but in which he have forget to make a room .
At least they suppose that he have forget this very important thing .
He must have , for there be n't any room .
It be a great joke .
They laugh a lot about it , and they lose a great deal of the respect for Paddy which they have have since he build his wonderful dam .
Jerry and Peter sit in the moonlight talk it over .
Paddy have stop bring stick for his wall .
He have dive down out of sight , and he be go a long time .
Suddenly Jerry notice that the water have grow very , very muddy all around Paddy 's new house .
He wrinkle his brow try to think what Paddy could be do .
Presently Paddy come up for air .
Then he go down again , and the water grow muddy than ever .
This go on for a long time .
Every little while Paddy would come up for air and a few minute of rest .
Then down he would go , and the water would grow muddy and muddier .
At last Jerry could stand it no longer .
He just have to see what be go on .
He slip into the water and swam over to where the water be muddy .
Just a he get there up come Paddy .
`` Hello , Cousin Jerry ! ''
say he .
`` I be just go to invite you over to see what you think of my house inside .
Just follow me . ''
Paddy dive , and Jerry dive after him .
He follow Paddy in at one of the three doorway under water and up a smooth hall right into the big , nice bedroom Jerry have ever see in all his life .
He just gasp in sheer surprise .
He could n't do anything else .
He could n't find his tongue to say a word .
Here he be in this splendid great room up above the water , and he have be so sure that there be n't any room at all !
He just do n't know what to make of it .
Paddy 's eye twinkle .
`` Well , '' say he , `` what do you think of it ? ''
`` I -- I -- think it be splendid , just perfectly splendid !
But I do n't understand it at all , Cousin Paddy .
I -- I -- Where be that great pile of mud I help you build in the middle ? ''
Jerry look as foolish a he felt when he ask this .
`` Why , I 've dig it all away .
That 's what make the water so muddy , '' reply Paddy .
`` But what do you build it for in the first place ? ''
Jerry ask .
`` Because I have to have something solid to rest my stick against while I be build my wall , of course , '' reply Paddy .
When I get the top fasten together for a roof , they do n't need a support any long , and then I dig it away to make this room .
I could n't have build such a big room any other way .
I see you do n't know very much about house-building , Cousin Jerry . ''
`` I -- I 'm afraid I do n't , '' confess Jerry sadly .
CHAPTER XIII The Queer Storehouse .
Everybody know that Paddy the Beaver be lay up a supply of food for the winter , and everybody think it be queer food .
That be , everybody but Prickly Porky the Porcupine think so .
Prickly Porky like the same kind of food , but he never lay up a supply .
He just go out and get it when he want it , winter or summer .
What kind of food be it ?
Why , bark , to be sure .
Yes , Sir , it be just bark -- the bark of certain kind of tree .
Now Prickly Porky can climb the tree and eat the bark right there , but Paddy the Beaver can not climb , and if he would just eat the bark that he can reach from the ground , it would take such a lot of tree to keep him fill up that he would soon spoil the Green Forest .
You know , when the bark be take off a tree all the way around , the tree die .
That be because all the thing that a tree draw out of the ground to make it grow and keep it alive be carry up from the root in the sap , and the sap can not go up the tree trunk and into the branch when the bark be take off , because it be up the inside of the bark that it travel .
So when the bark be take from a tree all the way around the trunk , the tree just starve to death .
Now Paddy the Beaver love the Green Forest as dearly a you and I do , and perhaps even a little more dearly .
You see , it be his home .
Besides , Paddy never be wasteful .
So he cut down a tree so that he can get all the bark instead of kill a whole lot of tree for a very little bark , a he might do if he be lazy .
There be n't a lazy bone in him -- not one .
The bark he like best be from the aspen .
When he can not get that , he will eat the bark from the poplar , the alder , the willow , and even the birch .
But he like the aspen so much good that he will work very hard to get it .
Perhaps it taste well because he do have to work so hard for it .
There be some aspen tree grow right on the edge of the pond Paddy have make in the Green Forest .
These he cut just a he have cut the tree for his dam .
As soon a a tree be down , he would cut it into short length , and with these swim out to where the water be deep , close to his new house .
He take them one by one and carry the first one to the bottom , where he push them into the mud just enough to hold them .
Then , a fast a he bring more , he pile them on the first one .
And so the pile grow and grow .
Jerry Muskrat , Peter Rabbit , Bobby Coon , and the other little people of the Green Forest watch him with the great interest and curiosity .
They could n't quite make out what he be do .
It be almost a if he be build the foundation for another house .
`` What 's he do , Jerry ? ''
demand Peter , when he could keep still no longer .
`` I do n't exactly know , '' reply Jerry .
`` He say that he be go to lay in a supply of food for the winter , just a I tell you , and I suppose that be what he be do .
But I do n't quite understand what he be take it all out into the pond for .
I believe I 'll go ask him . ''
`` Do , and then come tell u , '' beg Peter , who be grow so curious that he could n't sit still .
So Jerry swim out to where Paddy be so busy .
`` Is this your food supply , Cousin Paddy ? ''
he ask .
`` Yes , '' reply Paddy , crawl up on the side of his house to rest .
`` Yes , this be my food supply .
Is n't it splendid ? ''
`` I guess it be , '' reply Jerry , try to be polite , `` though I like lily root and clam well .
But what be you go to do with it ?
Where be your storehouse ? ''
`` This pond be my storehouse , '' reply Paddy .
`` I will make a great pile right here close to my house , and the water will keep it nice and fresh all winter .
When the pond be freeze over , all I will have to do be to slip out of one of my doorway down there on the bottom , swim over here and get a stick , and fill my stomach .
Is n't it handy ? ''
CHAPTER XIV A Footprint in the Mud .
Very early one morning Paddy the Beaver hear Sammy Jay make a terrible fuss over in the aspen tree on the edge of the pond Paddy have make in the Green Forest .
Paddy could n't see because he be inside his house , and it have no window , but he could hear .
He wrinkle up his brow thoughtfully .
`` Seems to me that Sammy be very much excite this morning , '' say he , a way he have because he be so much alone .
`` When he scream like that , Sammy be usually try to do two thing at once -- make trouble for somebody and keep somebody else out of trouble ; and when you come to think of it , that 's rather a funny way of do .
It show that he be n't all bad , and at the same time he be a long way from be all good .
Now , I should say from the sound that Sammy have discover Reddy Fox try to steal up on someone over where my aspen tree be grow .
Reddy be afraid of me , but I suspect that he know that Peter Rabbit have be hang around here a lot lately , watch me work , and he think perhaps he can watch Peter .
I shall have to whisper in one of Peter 's long ear and tell him to watch out . ''
After a while he hear Sammy Jay 's voice grow fainter and fainter in the Green Forest .
Finally he could n't hear it at all .
`` Whoever be here have go away , and Sammy have follow just to torment them , '' think Paddy .
He be very busy make a bed .
He be very particular about his bed , be Paddy the Beaver .
He make it of fine splinter of wood which he split off with those wonderful great cut teeth of his .
This make the dry kind of a bed .
It require a great deal of patience and work , but patience be one of the first thing a little Beaver learn , and honest work well do be one of the great pleasure in the world , a Paddy long ago find out for himself .
So he keep at work on his bed for some time after all be still outside .
At last Paddy decide that he would go over to his aspen tree and look them over to decide which one he would cut the next night .
He slide down one of his long hall , out the doorway at the bottom on the pond , and then swim up to the surface , where he float for a few minute with just his head out of water .
And all the time his eye and nose and ear be busy look , smell , and listen for any sign of danger .
Everything be still .
Sure that he be quite safe , Paddy swim across to the place where the aspen tree grow , and waddle out on the shore .
Paddy look this way and look that way .
He look up in the treetop , and he look off up the hill , but most of all he look at the ground .
Yes , Sir , Paddy just study the ground .
You see , he have n't forget the fuss Sammy Jay have be make there , and he be try to find out what it be all about .
At first he do n't see anything unusual , but by and by he happen to notice a little wet place , and right in the middle of it be something that make Paddy 's eye open wide .
It be a footprint !
Someone have carelessly step in the mud .
`` Ha ! ''
exclaim Paddy , and the hair on his back lift ever so little , and for a minute he have a prickly feeling all over .
The footprint be very much like that of Reddy Fox , only it be large .
`` Ha ! ''
say Paddy again .
`` That certainly be the foot print of Old Man Coyote !
I see I have get to watch out more sharply than I have think for .
All right , Mr. Coyote ; now that I know you be about , you 'll have to be smart than I think you be to catch me .
You certainly will be back here tonight look for me , so I think I 'll do my cut right now in the daytime . ''
CHAPTER XV Sammy Jay Makes Paddy a Call .
Paddy the Beaver be hard at work .
He have just cut down a good - size aspen tree and now he be gnaw it into short length to put in his food pile in the pond .
As he work , Paddy be do a lot of think about the footprint of Old Man Coyote in a little patch of mud , for he know that meant that Old Man Coyote have discover his pond , and would be hang around , hop to catch Paddy off his guard .
Paddy know it just as well a if Old Man Coyote have tell him so .
That be why he be at work cut his food supply in the daytime .
Usually he work at night , and he know that Old Man Coyote know it .
`` He 'll try to catch me then , '' think Paddy , `` so I 'll do my work on land now and fool him . ''
The tree he be cut begin to sway and crack .
Paddy cut out One more big chip , then hurry away to a safe place while the tree fell with a crash .
`` Thief !
thief !
thief ! ''
scream a voice just back of Paddy .
`` Hello , Sammy Jay !
I see you do n't feel any good than usual this morning , '' say Paddy .
`` Do n't you want to sit up in this tree while I cut it down ? ''
Sammy grow black in the face with anger , for he know that Paddy be laugh at him .
You remember how only a few day before he have be so intent on call Paddy bad name that he actually have n't notice that Paddy be cut the very tree in which he be sit , and so when it fell he have have a terrible fright .
`` You think you be very smart , Mr. Beaver , but you 'll think differently one of these fine day ! ''
scream Sammy .
`` If you know what I know , you would n't be so well satisfied with yourself . ''
`` What do you know ? ''
ask Paddy , pretend to be very much alarmed .
`` I 'm not go to tell you what I know , '' retort Sammy Jay .
`` You 'll find out soon enough .
And when you do find out , you 'll never steal another tree from our Green Forest .
Somebody be go to catch you , and it be n't Farmer Brown 's boy either ! ''
Paddy pretend to be terribly frighten .
`` Oh , who be it ?
Please tell me , Mr. Jay , '' he beg .
Now to be call Mr. Jay make Sammy feel very important .
Nearly everybody else call him Sammy .
He swell himself out try to look as important a he felt , and his eye snap with pleasure .
He be actually make Paddy the Beaver afraid .
At least , he think he be .
`` No , Sir , I wo n't tell you , '' he reply .
`` I would n't be you for a great deal , though !
Somebody who be smart than you be be go to catch you , and when he get through with you , there wo n't be anything left but a few bone .
No , Sir , nothing but a few bone ! ''
`` Oh , Mr. Jay , this be terrible news !
Whatever be I to do ? ''
cry Paddy , all the time keep on at work cut another tree .
`` There 's nothing you can do , '' reply Sammy , grin wickedly at Paddy 's fright .
`` There 's nothing you can do unless you go right straight back to the North where you come from .
You think you be very smart , but -- '' Sammy do n't finish .
Crack !
Over fell the tree Paddy have be cut and the top of it fell straight into the alder in which Sammy be sit .
`` Oh !
Oh !
Help ! ''
shriek Sammy , spread his wing and fly away just in time .
Paddy sit down and laugh until his side ache .
`` Come make me another call someday , Sammy ! ''
he say .
`` And when you do , please bring some real news .
I know all about Old Man Coyote .
You can tell him for me that when he be plan to catch people he should be careful not to leave footprint to give himself away . ''
Sammy do n't reply .
He just sneak off through the Green Forest , look quite as foolish a he felt .
CHAPTER XVI Old Man Coyote be Very Crafty .
Coyote have a crafty brain ; His wit be sharp his end to gain .
There be nothing in the world more true than that .
Old Man Coyote have the crafty brain of all the little people of the Green Forest or the Green Meadows .
Sharp a be the wit of old Granny Fox , they be not quite so sharp a the wit of Old Man Coyote .
If you want to fool him , you will have to get up very early in the morning , and then it be more than likely that you will be the one fool , not he .
There be very little go on around him that he do n't know about .
But once in a while something escape him .
The come of Paddy the Beaver to the Green Forest be one of these thing .
He do n't know a thing about Paddy until Paddy have finish his dam and his house , and be cut his supply of food for the winter .
You see , it be this way : When the Merry Little Breezes of Old Mother West Wind first hear what be go on in the Green Forest and hurry around over the Green Meadows and through the Green Forest to spread the news , a be their way , they take the great pain not to even hint it to Old Man Coyote because they be afraid that he would make trouble and perhaps drive Paddy away .
The place that Paddy have choose to build his dam be so deep in the Green Forest that Old Man Coyote seldom go that way .
So it be that he know nothing about Paddy , and Paddy know nothing about him for some time .
But after awhile Old Man Coyote notice that the little people of the Green Meadows be not about as much a usual .
They seem to have a secret of some kind .
He mention the matter to his friend , Digger the Badger .
Digger have be so intent on his own affair that he have n't notice anything unusual , but when Old Man Coyote mention the matter he remember that Blacky the Crow head straight for the Green Forest every morning .
Several time he have see Sammy Jay fly in the same direction a if in a great hurry to get somewhere .
Old Man Coyote grin .
`` That 's all I need to know , friend Digger , '' say he .
`` When Blacky the Crow and Sammy Jay visit a place more than once , something interesting be go on there .
I think I 'll take a stroll up through the Green Forest and have a look around . ''
With that , off Old Man Coyote start .
But he be too sly and crafty to go straight to the Green Forest .
He pretend to hunt around over the Green Meadows just a he usually do , all the time work nearer and nearer to the Green Forest .
When he reach the edge of it , he slip in among the tree , and when he felt that no one be likely to see him , he begin to run this way and that way with his nose to the ground .
`` Ha ! ''
he exclaim presently , `` Reddy Fox have be this way lately . ''
Pretty soon he find another trail .
`` So , '' say he , `` Peter Rabbit have be over here a good deal of late , and his trail go in the same direction a that of Reddy Fox .
I guess all I have to do now be to follow Peter 's trail , and it will lead me to what I want to find out . ''
So Old Man Coyote follow Peter 's trail , and he presently come to the pond of Paddy the Beaver .
`` Ha ! ''
say he , a he look out and saw Paddy 's new house .
`` So there be a newcomer to the Green Forest !
I have always hear that Beaver be very good eating .
My stomach begin to feel empty this very minute . ''
His mouth begin to water , and a fierce , hungry look shone in his eye .
It be just then that Sammy Jay saw him and begin to scream at the top of his lung so that Paddy the Beaver over in his house hear him .
Old Man Coyote know that it be of no use to stay longer with Sammy Jay about , so he take a hasty look at the pond and find where Paddy come ashore to cut his food .
Then , shake his fist at Sammy Jay , he start straight back for the Green Meadows .
`` I 'll just pay a visit here in the night , '' say he , `` and give Mr. Beaver a surprise while he be at work . ''
But with all his craft , Old Man Coyote do n't notice that he leave a footprint in the mud .
CHAPTER XVII Old Man Coyote be Disappointed .
Old Man Coyote lay stretch out in his favorite napping place on the Green Meadows .
He be think of what he have find out up in the Green Forest that morning -- that Paddy the Beaver be live there .
Old Man Coyote 's thought seem very pleasant to himself , though really they be very dreadful thought .
You see , he be think how easy it be go to be to catch Paddy the Beaver , and what a splendid meal he would make .
He lick his chop at the thought .
`` He do n't know I know he 's here , '' think Old Man Coyote .
`` In fact , I do n't believe heaven know that I be anywhere around .
Of course he wo n't be watch for me .
He cut his tree at night , so all I will have to do be to hide right close by where he be at work , and he 'll walk right into my mouth .
Sammy Jay know I be up there this morning , but Sammy sleep at night , so he will not give the alarm .
My , my , how good that Beaver will taste ! ''
He lick his chop once more , then yawn and close his eye for a nap .
Old Man Coyote wait until jolly , round red Mr. Sun have go to bed behind the Purple Hills , and the Black Shadows have creep out across the Green Meadows .
Then , keep in the blackest of them , and look very much like a shadow of himself , he slip into the Green Forest .
It be dark in there , and he make straight for Paddy 's new pond , trot along swiftly without make a sound .
When he be near the aspen tree which he know Paddy be plan to cut , he creep forward very slowly and carefully .
Everything be still a still could be .
`` Good ! ''
think Old Man Coyote .
`` I be here first , and now all I need do be to hide and wait for Paddy to come ashore . ''
So he stretch himself flat behind some brush close beside the little path Paddy have make up from the edge of the water and wait .
It be very still , so still that it seem almost a if he could hear his heart beat .
He could see the little star twinkle in the sky and their own reflection twinkle back at them from the water of Paddy 's pond .
Old Man Coyote wait and wait .
He be very patient when there be something to gain by it .
For such a splendid dinner a Paddy the Beaver would make , he felt that he could well afford to be patient .
So he wait and wait , and everything be as still a if no living thing but the tree where there .
Even the tree seem to be asleep .
At last , after a long , long time , he hear just the faint splash .
He prick up his ear and peep out on the pond with the hungry look in his yellow eye .
There be a little line of silver come straight toward him .
He know that it be make by Paddy the Beaver swimming .
Nearer and nearer it draw .
Old Man Coyote chuckle way down deep inside , without make a sound .
He could see Paddy 's head now , and Paddy be come straight in , a if he have n't a fear in the world .
Almost to the edge of the pond swam Paddy .
Then he stop .
In a few minute he begin to swim again , but this time it be back in the direction of his house , and he seem to be carry something .
It be one of the little food log he have cut that day , and he be take it out to his storehouse .
Then back he come for another .
And so he keep on , never once come ashore .
Old Man Coyote wait until Paddy have carry the last log to his storehouse and then , with a loud whack on the water with his broad tail , have dive and disappear in his house .
Then Old Man Coyote arise and start elsewhere to look for his dinner , and in his heart be bitter disappointment .
CHAPTER XVIII Old Man Coyote Tries Another Plan .
For three night Old Man Coyote have steal up through the green Forest with the come of the Black Shadows and have hide among the aspen tree where Paddy the Beaver cut his food , and for three night Paddy have fail to come ashore .
Each night he have seem to have enough food log in the water to keep him busy without cut more .
Old Man Coyote lay there , and the hungry look in his eye change to one of doubt and then to suspicion .
Could it be that Paddy the Beaver be smarter than he think ?
It begin to look very much a if Paddy know perfectly well that he be hide there each night .
Yes , Sir , that 's the way it look .
For three night Paddy have n't cut a single tree , and yet each night he have plenty of food log ready to take to his storehouse in the pond .
`` That mean that he come ashore in the daytime and cut his tree , '' think Old Man Coyote a , tire and with black anger in his heart , he trot home the third night .
`` He could n't have find out about me himself ; he be n't smart enough .
It must be that someone have tell him .
And nobody know that I have be over there but Sammy Jay .
It must be he who have be the tattletale .
I think I 'll visit Paddy by daylight tomorrow , and then we 'll see ! ''
Now the trouble with some smart people be that they be never able to believe that others may be as smart a they .
Old Man Coyote do n't know that the first time he have visit Paddy 's pond he have leave behind him a footprint in a little patch of soft mud .
If he have know it , he would n't have believe that Paddy would be smart enough to guess what that footprint meant .
So Old Man coyote lay all the blame at the door of Sammy Jay , and that very morning , when Sammy come fly over the Green Meadows , Old Man Coyote accuse him of be a tattletale and threaten the most dreadful thing to Sammy if ever he catch him .
Now Sammy have fly down to the green Meadows to tell Old Man Coyote how Paddy be do all his work on land in the daytime .
But when Old Man Coyote begin to call him a tattletale and accuse him of have warn Paddy , and to threaten dreadful thing , he straightway forget all his anger at Paddy and turn it all on Old Man Coyote .
He call him everything he could think of , and this be a great deal , for Sammy have a wicked tongue .
When he have n't any breath left , he fly over to the Green Forest , and there he hide where he could watch all that be go on .
That afternoon Old Man Coyote try his new plan .
He slip into the Green Forest , look this way and that way to be sure that no one saw him .
Then very , very softly , he creep up through the Green Forest toward the pond of Paddy the Beaver .
As he draw near , he hear a crash , and it make him smile .
He know what it mean .
It mean that Paddy be at work cut down tree .
With his stomach almost on the ground , he creep forward little by little , little by little , take the great care not to rustle so much a a leaf .
Presently he reach a place where he could see the aspen tree , and there , sure enough , be Paddy , sit up on his hind leg and hard at work cut another tree .
Old Man Coyote lay down for a few minute to watch .
Then he wriggle a little nearer .
Slowly and carefully he draw his leg under him and make ready for a rush .
Paddy the Beaver be his at last !
At just that very minute a harsh scream rang out right over his head : `` Thief !
thief !
thief ! ''
It be Sammy Jay , who have follow him all the way .
Paddy the Beaver do n't stop to even look around .
He know what that meant , and he scramble down his little path to the water a he never have scramble before .
And a he dive with a great splash , Old Man Coyote land with a great jump on the very edge of the pond .
CHAPTER XIX Paddy and Sammy Jay Become Friends .
Paddy the Beaver float in his pond and grin in the most provoking way at Old Man Coyote , who have so nearly catch him .
Old Man Coyote fairly dance with anger on the bank .
He have felt so sure of Paddy that time that it be hard work to believe that Paddy have really get away from him .
He bar his long , cruel teeth , and he look very fierce and ugly .
`` Come on in ; the water 's fine ! ''
call Paddy .
Now , of course this be n't a nice thing for Paddy to do , for it only make Old Man Coyote all the angrier .
You see , Paddy know perfectly well that he be absolutely safe , and he just could n't resist the temptation to say some unkind thing .
He have have to be on the watch for day l he should be catch , and so he have n't be able to work quite so well a he could have do with nothing to fear , and he still have a lot of preparation to make for winter .
So he tell Old Man Coyote just what he think of him , and that he be n't as smart a he think he be or he never would have leave a foot print in the mud to give him away .
When Sammy Jay , who be listen and chuckle a he listen , heard that , he fly down where he would be just out of reach of Old Man Coyote , and then he just turn that tongue of his loose , and you know that some people say that Sammy 's tongue be hang in the middle and wag at both end .
Of course this be n't really so , but when he get to abuse people it seem a if it must be true .
He call Old Man Coyote every bad name he could think of .
He call him a sneak , a thief , a coward , a bully , and a lot of other thing .
`` You say I have warn Paddy that you be try to catch him and that be why you fail to find him at work at night , and all the time you have warn him yourself ! ''
scream Sammy .
`` I use to think that you be smart , but I know well now .
Paddy be twice as smart a you be .
`` Mr. Coyote be every so sly ; Mr. Coyote be clever and spry ; If you believe all you hear .
Mr. Coyote be naught of the kind ; Mr. Coyote be stupid and blind ; He ca n't catch a flea on his ear . ''
Paddy the Beaver laugh till the tear come at Sammy 's foolish verse , but it make Old Man Coyote angrier than ever .
He be angry with Paddy for escape from him , and he be angry with Sammy , terribly angry , and the bad of it be he could n't catch either one , for one be at home in the water and the other be at home in the air and he could n't follow in either place .
Finally he saw it be of no use to stay there to be laugh at , so , mutter and grumbling , he start for the Green Meadows .
As soon a he be out of sight Paddy turn to Sammy Jay .
`` Mr. Jay , '' say he , know how it please Sammy to be call mister .
`` Mr. Jay , you have do me a mighty good turn today , and I be not go to forget it .
You can call me what you please and scream at me all you please , but you wo n't get any satisfaction out of it , because I simply wo n't get angry .
I will say to myself , ` Mr. Jay save my life the other day , ' and then I wo n't mind your tongue . ''
Now this make Sammy feel very proud and very happy .
You know it be very seldom that he hear anything nice say of him .
He fly down on the stump of one of the tree Paddy have cut .
`` Let 's be friend , '' say he .
`` With all my heart ! ''
reply Paddy .
CHAPTER XX Sammy Jay Offers To Help Paddy .
Paddy sit look thoughtfully at the aspen tree he would have to cut to complete his store of food for the winter .
All those near the edge of his pond have be cut .
The others be scatter about some little distance away .
`` I do n't know , '' say Paddy out loud .
`` I do n't know . ''
`` What do n't you know ? ''
ask Sammy Jay , who , now that he and Paddy have become friend , be very much interested in what Paddy be do .
`` Why , '' reply Paddy , `` I do n't know just how I be go to get those tree .
Now that Old Man Coyote be watch for me , it be n't safe for me to go very far from my pond .
I suppose I could dig a canal up to some of the near tree and then float them down to the pond , but it be hard to work and keep watch for enemy at the same time .
I guess I 'll have to be content with some of these alder grow close to the water , but he bark of aspen be so much good that I -- I wish I could get them . ''
`` What 's a canal ? ''
ask Sammy abruptly .
`` A canal ?
Why a canal be a kind of ditch in which water can run , '' reply Paddy .
Sammy nod .
`` I 've see Farmer Brown dig one over on the Green Meadows , but it look like a great deal of work .
I do n't suppose that anyone else could do it .
Do you really mean that you can dig a canal , Paddy ? ''
`` Of course I mean it , '' reply Paddy , in a surprised tone of voice .
`` I have help dig lot of canal .
You ought to see some of them back where I come from . ''
`` I 'd like to , '' reply Sammy .
`` I think it be perfectly wonderful .
I do n't see how you do it . ''
`` It 's easy enough when you know how , '' reply Paddy .
`` If I dare to , I 'd show you . ''
Sammy have a sudden idea .
It almost make him gasp .
`` I tell you what , you work and I 'll keep watch ! ''
he cry .
`` You know my eye be very sharp . ''
`` Will you ? ''
cry Paddy eagerly .
`` That would be perfectly splendid .
You have the sharp eye of anyone whom I know , and I would feel perfectly safe with you on watch .
But I do n't want to put you to all to that trouble , Mr. Jay . ''
`` Of course I will , '' reply Sammy , `` and it wo n't be any trouble at all .
I 'll just love to do it . ''
You see , it make Sammy feel very proud to have Paddy say that he have such sharp eye .
`` When will you begin ? ''
`` Right away , if you will just take a look around and see that it be perfectly safe for me to come out on land . ''
Sammy do n't wait to hear more .
He spread his beautiful blue wing and start off over the Green Forest straight for the Green Meadows .
Paddy watch him go with a puzzled and disappointed air .
`` That 's funny , '' think he .
`` I think he really mean it , and now off he go without even say good-by . ''
In a little while back come Sammy , all out of breath .
`` It 's all right , '' he pant .
`` You can go to work just as soon a you please . ''
Paddy look more puzzled than ever .
`` How do you know ? ''
he ask .
`` I have n't see you look around . ''
`` I do good than that , '' reply Sammy .
`` If Old Man Coyote have be hide somewhere in the Green Forest , it might have take me some time to find him .
But he be n't .
You see , I fly straight over to his home in the Green Meadows to see if he be there , and he be .
He 's take a sun bath and look as cross a two stick .
I do n't think he 'll be back here this morning , but I 'll keep a sharp watch while you work . ''
Paddy make Sammy a low bow .
`` You certainly be smart , Mr. Jay , '' say he .
`` I would n't have think of go over to Old Man Coyote 's home to see if he be there .
I 'll feel perfectly safe with you on guard .
Now I 'll get to work . ''
CHAPTER XXI Paddy and Sammy Jay Work Together .
Jerry Muskrat have be home at the Smiling Pool for several day .
But he could n't stay there long .
Oh , my , no !
He just have to get back to see what his big cousin , Paddy the Beaver , be do .
So as soon a he be sure that everything be all right at the Smiling Pool he hurry back up the Laughing Brook to Paddy 's pond , deep in the Green Forest .
As soon a he be in sight of it , he look eagerly for Paddy .
At first he do n't see him .
Then he stop and gaze over at the place where Paddy have be cut aspen tree for food .
Something be go on there , something queer .
He could n't make it out .
Jus then Sammy Jay come fly over .
`` What 's Paddy do ? ''
Jerry ask .
Sammy Jay drop down to the top of an alder tree and fluff out all his feather in a very important way .
`` Oh , '' say he , `` Paddy and I be build something ! ''
`` You !
Paddy and you !
Ha , ha !
Paddy and you build something ! ''
Jerry laugh .
`` Yes , me ! ''
snap Sammy angrily .
`` That 's what I say ; Paddy and I be build something . ''
Jerry have begin to swim across the pond by this time , and Sammy be fly across .
`` Why do n't you tell the truth , Sammy , and say that Paddy be build something and you be make him all the trouble you can ? ''
call Jerry .
Sammy 's eye snap angrily , and he dart down at Jerry 's little brown head .
`` It be n't true ! ''
he shriek .
`` You ask Paddy if I 'm not help ! ''
Jerry duck under water to escape Sammy 's sharp bill .
When he come up again , Sammy be over in the little grove of aspen tree where Paddy be at work .
Then Jerry discover something .
What be it ?
Why a little water-path lead right up to the aspen tree , and there , at the end of the little water-path , be Paddy the Beaver hard at work .
He be dig and pile the earth on one side very neatly .
In fact , he be make the water-path longer .
Jerry swam right up the little water-path to where Paddy be work .
`` Good morning , Cousin Paddy , '' say he .
`` What be you do ? ''
`` Oh , '' reply Paddy , `` Sammy Jay and I be build a canal . ''
Sammy Jay look down at Jerry in triumph , and Jerry look at Paddy a if he think that he be joke .
`` Sammy Jay ?
What 's Sammy Jay get to do about it ? ''
demand Jerry .
`` A whole lot , '' reply Paddy .
`` You see , he keep watch while I work .
If he do n't , I could n't work , and there would n't be any canal .
Old Man Coyote have be try to catch me , and I would n't dare work on shore if it be n't that I be sure that the sharp eye in the Green Forest be watch for danger . ''
Sammy Jay look very much pleased indeed and very proud .
`` So you see , it take both of u to make this canal ; I dig while Sammy watch .
So we be build it together , '' conclude Paddy with a twinkle in his eye .
`` I see , '' say Jerry slowly .
Then he turn to Sammy Jay .
`` I beg your pardon , Sammy , '' say he .
`` I do indeed . ''
`` That 's all right , '' reply Sammy airily .
`` What do you think of our canal ? ''
`` I think it be wonderful , '' reply Jerry .
And indeed it be a very fine canal , straight , wide , and deep enough for Paddy to swim in and float his log out to the pond .
Yes , indeed , it be a very fine canal .
CHAPTER XXII Paddy Finishes His Harvest .
`` Sharp his tongue and sharp his eye -- Sammy guard against surprise .
If ` twere not for Sammy Jay I could do no work today . ''
When Sammy overheard Paddy the Beaver say that to Jerry Muskrat , it make him swell up all over with pure pride .
You see , Sammy be so used to hear bad thing about himself that to hear something nice like that please him immensely .
He straightway forget all the mean thing he have say to Paddy when he first saw him -- how he have call him a thief because he have cut the aspen tree he need .
He forget all this .
He forget how Paddy have make him the laughingstock of the Green Forest and the Green Meadows by cut down the very tree in which he have be sit .
He forget everything but that Paddy have trust him to keep watch and now be say nice thing about him .
He make up his mind that he would deserve all the nice thing that Paddy could say , and he think that Paddy be the fine fellow in the world .
Jerry Muskrat look doubtful .
He do n't trust Sammy , and he take care not to go far from the water when he hear that Old Man Coyote have be hang around .
But Paddy work away just a if he have n't a fear in the world .
`` The way to make people want to be trust be to trust them '' say he to himself .
`` If I show Sammy Jay that I do n't really trust him , he will think it be of no use to try and will give it up .
But if I do trust him , and he know that I do , he 'll be the best watchman in the Green Forest . ''
And this show that Paddy the Beaver have a great deal of wisdom , for it be just a he think .
Sammy be on hand bright and early every morning .
He make sure that Old Man Coyote be nowhere in the Green Forest , and then he settle himself comfortably in the top of a tall pine tree where he could see all that be go on while Paddy the Beaver work .
Paddy have finish his canal , and a beautiful canal it be , lead straight from his pond up to the aspen tree .
As soon a he have finish it , he begin to cut the tree .
As soon a one be down he would cut it into short length and roll them into the canal .
Then he would float them out to his pond and over to his storehouse .
He take the large branch , on which there be sweet , tender bark , in the same way , for Paddy be never wasteful .
After a while he go over to his storehouse , which , you know , be nothing but a great pile of aspen log and branch in his pond close by his house .
He study it very carefully .
Then he swim back and climb up on the bank of his canal .
`` Mr. Jay , '' say he , `` I think our work be about finish . ''
`` What ! ''
cry Sammy , `` Are n't you go to cut the rest of those aspen tree ? ''
`` No , '' reply Paddy .
`` Enough be always enough , and I 've get enough to last me all winter .
I want those tree for next year .
Now I be fix for the winter .
I think I 'll take it easy for a while . ''
Sammy look disappointed .
You see , he have just begin to learn that the great pleasure in the world come from do thing for other people .
For the first time since he could remember , someone want him around land it give him such a good feeling down deep inside !
Perhaps it be because he remember that good feeling that the next spring he be so willing and anxious to help poor Mrs. Quack .
