Reddy hang his head .

Suddenly Granny Fox lift her head .
`` Hark ! ''

`` Now , Reddy , you run across the bridge and watch from the top of the little hill over there .

Reddy trot across the long bridge and up to the top of the hill , a Granny have tell him to .
Then he sit down to watch .
Granny trot out in the middle of a field and sit down .

Reddy do not know what to make of it , for Granny seem simply to be play with the hound and not really try to get away from him at all .
Pretty soon Reddy hear another sound .
It be a long , low rumble .
Then there be a distant whistle .
It be a train .
Granny hear it , too .
As she run , she begin to work back toward the long bridge .
The train be in sight now .
Suddenly Granny Fox start across the bridge so fast that she look like a little red streak .
The dog be close at her heel when she start and he be so eager to catch her that he do n't see either the bridge or the train .
But he could n't begin to run as fast a Granny Fox .
Oh , my , no !
When she have reach the other side , he be n't halfway across , and right behind him , whistle for him to get out of the way , be the train .
The hound give one frightened yelp , and then he do the only thing he could do ; he leap down , down into the swift water below , and the last Reddy saw of him he be frantically try to swim ashore .
`` Now you know why I want you to learn to cross a bridge ; it 's a very nice way of get rid of dog , '' say Granny Fox , a she climb up beside Reddy .
III .
Bowser the Hound Is n't Fooled Reddy Fox have be teach so much by Granny Fox that he begin to feel very wise and very important .
Reddy be naturally smart and he have be very quick to learn the trick that old Granny Fox have teach him .
But Reddy Fox be a boaster .
Every day he swagger about on the Green Meadows and brag how smart he be .
Blacky the Crow grow tire of Reddy 's boasting .
`` If you 're so smart , what be the reason you always keep out of sight of Bowser the Hound ? ''
ask Blacky .
`` For my part , I do n't believe that you be smart enough to fool him . ''
A lot of little meadow people hear Blacky say this , and Reddy know it .
He also know that if he do n't prove Blacky in the wrong he would be laugh at forever after .
Suddenly he remember the trick that Granny Fox have play on the young hound at the railroad bridge .
Why not play the same trick on Bowser and invite Blacky the Crow to see him do it ?
He would .
`` If you will be over at the railroad bridge when the train come this afternoon , I 'll show you how easy it be to fool Bowser the Hound , '' say Reddy .
Blacky agree to be there , and Reddy start off to find out where Bowser be .
Blacky tell everyone he meet how Reddy Fox have promise to fool Bowser the Hound , and every time he tell it he chuckle as if he think it the best joke ever .
Blacky the Crow be on hand promptly that afternoon and with him come his cousin , Sammy Jay .

Just a old Granny Fox have do with the young hound , Reddy allow Bowser to get very near him and then , a the train come roar along , he race across the long bridge just ahead of it .
He have think that Bowser would be so intent on catch him that he would not notice the train until he be on the bridge and it be too late , a have be the case with the young hound .

The train be halfway across the bridge , but Bowser be nowhere to be see .
He must have jump already .

`` Haw , haw , haw !
How smart we be ! ''
It be Blacky the Crow .
IV .
Reddy Fox Grows Bold Reddy Fox be grow bold .
Everybody say so , and what everybody say must be so .
Reddy Fox have always be very sly and not bold at all .
The truth be Reddy Fox have so many time fool Bowser the Hound and Farmer Brown 's boy that he have begin to think himself very smart indeed .
He have really fool himself .
Yes , Sir , Reddy Fox have fool himself .

Now it be one of the bad habit in the world to think too much of one 's self .

Oh , my , yes !
Reddy Fox certainly do have the habit !

Yes , Sir , Reddy Fox have grow careless .

VI .
Drummer the Woodpecker Drums in Vain Once upon a time , before he have grow to think himself so very , very smart , Reddy Fox would never , never have think of run without watch out in every direction .

Now everybody who hear that rat-a-tat-tat-tat know that it be a danger signal .
Drummer the Woodpecker never drum just that way for pleasure .

He do n't notice it at all .

I surely would ! ''

VII .
Too Late Reddy Fox Hears Drummer the Woodpecker be pound out his danger signal so fast and so hard that his red head fly back and forth almost too fast to see .
Rat-a-tat-tat-a-tat-tat , beat Drummer on the old tree trunk on the edge of the Green Forest .

So Drummer the Woodpecker crept around to the other side of the tree and in a minute be drum hard than ever .

Now Reddy Fox have grow as careless a he have grow bold .

My , my , indeed he have !

For just a wee little second it seem to Reddy Fox that his heart stop beat .

Reddy 's sharp eye saw Drummer the Woodpecker near the top of the old tree trunk and notice that Drummer seem to be look at something down below .

Reddy Fox give a little gasp of fright and turn so suddenly that he almost fell flat .

It seem a though his fly foot hardly touch the grass .

Bang !
Bang !
Two flash of fire and two puff of smoke dart from behind the old tree trunk .
Drummer the Woodpecker give a frightened scream and flew deep into the Green Forest .
Peter Rabbit flatten himself under a friendly bramble bush .

VIII .
Granny Fox Takes Care of Reddy Reddy Fox be so sore and lame that he could hardly hobble .

Oh , my , no !
There be nothing gentle about that !

`` A little Fox must use his eye Or get someday a sad surprise .
`` A little Fox must use his ear And know what make each sound he hear .
`` A little Fox must use his nose And try the wind where'er he go .
`` A little Fox must use all three To live to grow as old a me .
`` Now tell me all about it , Reddy Fox .

IX .
Peter Rabbit Hears the News Johnny Chuck come run up to the edge of the Old Briarpatch quite out of breath .

`` All right , '' say Johnny Chuck , and off they start .
X . Poor Reddy Fox Peter Rabbit and Johnny Chuck steal up the hill toward the home of Reddy Fox .
As they draw near , they creep from one bunch of grass to another and from bush to bush , stop behind each to look and listen .
They be not take any chance .
Johnny Chuck be not much afraid of Reddy Fox , for he have whip him once , but he be afraid of old Granny Fox .
Peter Rabbit be afraid of both .
The nearer he get to the home of Reddy Fox , the more anxious and nervous he grow .
You see , Reddy Fox have play so many trick to try and catch Peter that Peter be not quite sure that this be not another trick .
So he keep a sharp watch in every direction , ready to run at the least sign of danger .
When they have tiptoe and crawl to a point where they could see the doorstep of the Fox home , Peter Rabbit and Johnny Chuck lay down in a clump of bush and watch .
Pretty soon they saw old Granny Fox come out .
She sniff the wind and then she start off at a quick run down the Lone Little Path .
Johnny Chuck give a sigh of relief , for he be n't afraid of Reddy and now he felt safe .
But Peter Rabbit be just as watchful a ever .
`` I 've get to see Reddy for myself before I 'll go a step nearer , '' he whisper .
Just then Johnny Chuck put a hand on his lip and point with the other hand .
There be Reddy Fox crawl out of his doorway into the sun .
Peter Rabbit lean forward to see good .
Was Reddy Fox really so badly hurt , or be he only pretend ?
Reddy Fox crawl painfully out onto his doorstep .
He try to stand and walk , but he could n't because he be too stiff and sore .
So he just crawl .
He do n't know that anyone be watch him , and with every movement he make a face .
That be because it hurt so .
Peter Rabbit , watch from the clump of bush , know then that Reddy be not pretend .
He know that he have nothing , not the least little thing , to fear from Reddy Fox .
So Peter give a whoop of joy and spring out into view .
Reddy look up and try to grin , but make a face of pain instead .
You see , it hurt so to move .
`` I suppose you 're tickle to death to see me like this , '' he growl to Peter Rabbit .
Now Peter have every reason to be glad , for Reddy Fox have try his best to catch Peter Rabbit to give to old Granny Fox for her dinner , and time and again Peter have just barely escape .
So at first Peter Rabbit have whoop with joy .
But a he saw how very helpless Reddy really be and how much pain he felt , suddenly Peter Rabbit 's big , soft eye fill with tear of pity .
He forget all about the threat of Reddy Fox and how Reddy have try to trick him .
He forget all about how mean Reddy have be .
`` Poor Reddy Fox , '' say Peter Rabbit .
`` Poor Reddy Fox . ''
XI .
Granny Fox Returns Up over the hill trot old Granny Fox .
She be on her way home with a tender young chicken for Reddy Fox .
Poor Reddy !
Of course , it be his own fault , for he have be show off and he have be careless or he never would have go so near to the old tree trunk behind which Farmer Brown 's boy be hide .
But old Granny Fox do n't know this .
She never make such mistake herself .
Oh , my , no !
So now , a she come up over the hill to a place where she could see her home , she lay the chicken down and then she creep behind a little bush and look all over the Green Meadows to see if the way be clear .
She know that Bowser the Hound be chain up .
She have see Farmer Brown and Farmer Brown 's boy hoeing in the cornfield , so she have nothing to fear from them .
Looking over to her doorstep , she saw Reddy Fox lie in the sun , and then she saw something else , something that make her eye flash and her teeth come together with a snap .
It be Peter Rabbit sit up very straight , not ten foot from Reddy Fox .
`` So that 's that young scamp of a Peter Rabbit whom Reddy be go to catch for me when I be sick and could n't !
I 'll just show Reddy Fox how easily it can be do , and he shall have tender young rabbit with his chicken ! ''
say Granny Fox to herself .
So first she study and study every clump of grass and every bush behind which she could creep .
She saw that she could get almost to where Peter Rabbit be sit and never once show herself to him .
Then she look this way and look that way to make sure that no one be watch her .
No one do she see on the Green Meadows who be look her way .
Then Granny Fox begin to crawl from one clump of grass to another and from bush to bush .
Sometimes she wriggle along flat on her stomach .
Little by little she be draw nearer and nearer to Peter Rabbit .
Now with all her smartness old Granny Fox have forget one thing .
Yes , Sir , she have forget one thing .
Never once have she think to look up in the sky .
And there be Ol ' Mistah Buzzard sail round and round and look down and see all that be go on below .
Ol ' Mistah Buzzard be sharp .
He know just what old Granny Fox be plan to do -- know it as well a if he have read her thought .
His eye twinkle .
`` Ah cert ` nly ca n't allow li'l ' Brer Rabbit to be hurt , Ah cert ` nly ca n't ! ''
mutter Ol ' Mistah Buzzard , and chuckle .
Then he slant his broad wing downward and without a sound slide down out of the sky till he be right behind Granny Fox .
`` Do yo ' always crawl home , Granny Fox ? ''
ask Ol ' Mistah Buzzard .
Granny Fox be so startled , for she have n't hear a sound , that she jump almost out of her skin .
Of course Peter Rabbit saw her then , and be off like a shot .
Granny Fox show all her teeth .
`` I wish you would mind your own business , Mistah Buzzard ! ''
she snarl .
`` Cert ` nly , cert ` nly , Ah sho ` ly will ! ''
reply Ol ' Mistah Buzzard , and sail up into the blue , blue sky .
XII .
The Lost Chicken When old Granny Fox have lay down the chicken she be bring home to Reddy Fox to try to catch Peter Rabbit , she have mean to go right back and get it as soon a she have catch Peter .
Now she saw Peter go across the Green Meadows , lipperty-lipperty-lip , a fast a he could go .
She be so angry that she hop up and down .
She tear up the grass and ground her long , white teeth .
She glare up at Ol ' Mistah Buzzard , who have warn Peter Rabbit , but all she could do be to scold , and that do n't do her much good , for in a few minute Ol ' Mistah Buzzard be so far up in the blue , blue sky that he could n't hear a word she be say .
My , my , but old Granny Fox certainly be angry !
If she have n't be so angry she might have see Johnny Chuck lie as flat a he could make himself behind a big clump of grass .
Johnny Chuck be scar .
Yes , indeed , Johnny Chuck be dreadfully scar .
He have fight Reddy Fox and whip him , but he know that old Granny Fox would be too much for him .
So it be with great relief that Johnny Chuck saw her stop tearing up the grass and trot over to see how Reddy Fox be get along .
Then Johnny Chuck creep along until he be far enough away to run .
How he do run !
He be so fat and roly-poly that he be all out of breath when he reach home , and so tire that he just drop down on his doorstep and pant .
`` Serves me right for have so much curiosity , '' say Johnny Chuck to himself .
Reddy Fox look up a old Granny Fox come hurry home .
He be weak and very , very hungry .
But he felt sure that old Granny Fox would bring him something nice for his breakfast , and as soon a he hear her footsteps his mouth begin to water .
`` Did you bring me something nice , Granny ? ''
ask Reddy Fox .
Now old Granny Fox have be so put out by the scare she have have and by her failure to catch Peter Rabbit that she have forget all about the chicken she have leave up on the hill .
When Reddy speak , she remember it , and the thought of have to go way back after it do n't improve her temper a bit .
`` No ! ''
she snap .
`` I have n't !
-- You do n't deserve any breakfast anyway .
If you have any gumption '' -- that 's the word Granny Fox use , gumption -- `` if you have any gumption at all , you would n't have get in trouble , and could get your own breakfast . ''
Reddy Fox do n't know what gumption meant , but he do know that he be very , very hungry , and do what he would , he could n't keep back a couple of big tear of disappointment .
Granny Fox saw them .
`` There , there , Reddy !
Do n't cry .
I 've get a fine fat chicken for you up on the hill , and I 'll run back and get it , '' say Granny Fox .
So off she start up the hill to the place where she have leave the chicken when she start to try to catch Peter Rabbit .
When she get there , there be n't any chicken .
No , Sir , there be no chicken at all -- just a few feather .
Granny Fox could hardly believe her own eye .
She look this way and she look that way , but there be no chicken , just a few feather .
Old Granny Fox fly into a great rage than before .
XIII .
Granny Fox Calls Jimmy Skunk Names Granny Fox could n't believe her own eye .
No , Sir , she could n't believe her own eye , and she rub them two or three time to make sure that she be see right .
That chicken certainly have disappear , and leave no trace of where it have go .
It be very queer .
Old Granny Fox sit down to think who would dare steal anything from her .
Then she walk in a big circle with her nose to the ground , sniff and sniff .
What be she do that for ?
Why , to see if she could find the track of anyone who might have steal her chicken .
`` Aha ! ''
exclaim old Granny Fox , start to run along the top of the hill , her nose to the ground .
`` Aha !
I 'll catch him this time ! ''
In a few minute she begin to run more slowly , and every two or three step she would look ahead .
Suddenly her eye snap , and she begin to creep almost flat on her stomach , just a she have crept for Peter Rabbit .
But it be n't Peter Rabbit this time .
It be -- who do you think ?
Jimmy Skunk !
Yes , Sir , it be Jimmy Skunk .
He be slowly amble along , for Jimmy Skunk never hurry .
Every big stick or stone that he could move , he would pull over or look under , for Jimmy Skunk be hunt for beetle .
Old Granny Fox watch him .
`` He must have a tremendous appetite to be hunt for beetle after eat my chicken ! ''
mutter she .
Then she jump out in front of Jimmy Skunk , her eye snapping , her teeth showing , and the hair on her back stand on end so a to make her look very fierce .
But all the time old Granny Fox take the great care not to get too near to Jimmy Skunk .
`` Where 's my chicken ? ''
snarl old Granny Fox , and she look very , very fierce .
Jimmy Skunk look up a if very much surprise .
`` Hello , Granny Fox ! ''
he exclaim .
`` Have you lose a chicken ? ''
`` You 've steal it !
You 're a thief , Jimmy Skunk ! ''
snap Granny Fox .
`` Words can never make black white ; Before you speak be sure you 're right , '' say Jimmy Skunk .
`` I 'm not a thief . ''
`` You be ! ''
cry Granny work herself into a great rage .
`` I 'm not ! ''
`` You be ! ''
All the time Jimmy Skunk be chuckle to himself , and the more he chuckle the angrier grow old Granny Fox .
And all the time Jimmy Skunk keep move toward old Granny Fox and Granny Fox keep back away , for , like all the other little meadow and forest people , she have very great respect for Jimmy Skunk 's little bag of scent .
Now , back off that way , she could n't see where she be go , and the first thing she know she have back into a bramble bush .
It tear her skirt and scratch her leg .
`` Ooch ! ''
cry old Granny Fox .
`` Ha !
ha !
ha ! ''
laugh Jimmy Skunk .
`` That 's what you get for call me name . ''
XIV .
Granny Fox Finds What Became of the Chicken Old Granny Fox be in a terrible temper .
Dear , dear , it certainly be a dreadful temper !
Jimmy Skunk laugh at her , and that make it bad .
When he saw this , Jimmy Skunk just roll over and over on the ground and shout , he be so tickled .
Of course , it be n't the least bit nice of Jimmy Skunk , but you know that Granny Fox have be call Jimmy a thief .
Then Jimmy do n't like Granny Fox anyway , nor do any of the other little meadow and forest people , for most of them be very much afraid of her .
When old Granny Fox finally get out of the bramble bush , she do n't stop to say anything more to Jimmy Skunk , but hurry away , mutter and grumble and grind her teeth .
Old Granny Fox be n't pleasant to meet just then , and when Bobby Coon saw her coming , he just think it best to get out of her way , so he climb a tree .
It be n't that Bobby Coon be afraid of old Granny Fox .
Bless you , no !
Bobby Coon be n't a bit afraid of her .
It be because he have a full stomach and be feel too good-natured and lazy to quarrel .
`` Good morning , Granny Fox .
I hope you be feel well this morning , '' say Bobby Coon , a old Granny Fox come trot under the tree he be sit in .
Granny Fox look up and glare at him with yellow eye .
`` It be n't a good morning and I 'm not feel fine ! ''
she snap .
`` My goodness , how you have tear your skirt ! ''
exclaim Bobby Coon .
Old Granny Fox start to say something unpleasant .
Then she change her mind and instead she sit down and tell Bobby Coon all her trouble .
As she talk , Bobby Coon keep duck his head behind a branch of the tree to hide a smile .
Finally Granny Fox notice it .
`` What do you keep duck your head for , Bobby Coon ? ''
she ask suspiciously .
`` I 'm just look to see if I can see any feather from that chicken , '' reply Bobby Coon gravely , though his eye be twinkle with mischief .
`` Well , do you ? ''
demand old Granny Fox .
And just then Bobby Coon do .
They be not on the ground , however , but float in the air .
Bobby Coon lean out to see where they come from , and Granny Fox turn to look , too .
What do you think they saw ?
Why , sit on a tall , dead tree be Mr. Goshawk , just then swallow the last of Granny 's chicken .
`` Thief !
thief !
robber !
robber ! ''
shriek old Granny Fox .
But Mr. Goshawk say nothing , just wink at Bobby Coon , puff out his feather , and settle himself for a comfortable nap .
XV .
Reddy Fox Has a Visitor Hardly be old Granny Fox out of sight on her way to hunt for the chicken she have leave on the hill , when Unc ' Billy Possum come stroll along the Lone Little Path .
He be hum to himself , for he have just have a good breakfast .
One of the Merry Little Breezes spy him and hurry to meet him and tell him about how Reddy Fox have be shoot .
Unc ' Billy listen , and the grin with which he have greet the Merry Little Breeze grow into a broad smile .
`` Are yo ' all sure about that ? ''
he ask .
The Merry Little Breeze be sure .
Unc ' Billy Possum stop for a few minute and consider .
`` Serves that no ` count Reddy Fox right , '' chuckle Unc ' Billy .
`` He do spoil mah hunt at Farmer Brown 's , he raise such a fuss among the hen up there .
'T be n't safe to go there any mo ' !
No , Suh , 't be n't safe , and it wo n't be safe for a right smart while .
Did yo ' say that Granny Fox be home ? ''
The Merry Little Breeze have n't say anything about Granny Fox , but now remember that she have go up the hill .
`` Ah believe Ah will just tote my sympathy over to Reddy Fox , '' say Unc ' Billy Possum , a he start in the direction of Reddy Fox 's house .
But he make sure that old Granny Fox be not at home before he show himself .
Reddy Fox lay on his doorstep .
He be sick and sore and stiff .
Indeed , he be so stiff he could n't walk at all .
And he be weak -- weak and hungry , dreadfully hungry .
When he hear footstep , he think old Granny Fox be bring him the chicken after which she have go .
He felt too ill even to turn his head .
`` Did you get the chicken , Granny ? ''
he ask weakly .
No one answer .
`` I say , do you get the chicken , Granny ? ''
Reddy 's voice sound a little sharp and cross a he ask this time .
Still there be no reply , and Reddy begin to be a little bit suspicious .
He turn over and raise his head to look .
Instead of old Granny Fox , there be Unc ' Billy Possum grin at him .
`` Smarty , Smarty be a thief !
Smarty , Smarty come to grief !
Tried to show off just for fun And run too near a loaded gun .
`` Yo ' all certainly have get just what yo ' deserve , and Ah 'm glad of it !
Ah 'm glad of it , Suh ! ''
say Unc ' Billy Possum severely .
An angry light come into the eye of Reddy Fox and make them an ugly yellow for just a minute .
But he felt too sick to quarrel .
Unc ' Billy Possum saw this .
He saw how Reddy be really suffering , and down deep in his heart Unc ' Billy be truly sorry for him .
But he do n't let Reddy know it .
No , indeed !
He just pretend to be tickle to death to see Reddy Fox so helpless .
He do n't dare stay long , for fear Granny Fox would return .
So , after say a few more thing to make Reddy feel uncomfortable , Unc ' Billy start off up the Lone Little Path toward the Green Forest .
`` Too bad !
Too bad ! ''
he mutter to himself .
`` If ol ' Granny Fox be n't smart enough to get Reddy enough to eat , Ah 'll have to see what we-alls can do .
Ah cert ` nly will . ''
XVI .
Unc ' Billy Possum Visits the Smiling Pool Joe Otter and Billy Mink be sit on the Big Rock in the Smiling Pool .
Because they have nothing else to do , they be plan mischief .
Jerry Muskrat be busy fill his new house with food for the winter .
He be too busy to get into mischief .
Suddenly Billy Mink put a finger on his lip a a warning to Little Joe Otter to keep perfectly still .
Billy 's sharp eye have see something move over in the bulrush .
Together he and Little Joe Otter watch , ready to dive into the Smiling Pool at the first sign of danger .
In a few minute the rush part and a sharp little old face peer out .
Little Joe Otter and Billy Mink each sigh with relief , and their eye begin to dance .
`` Hi , Unc ' Billy Possum ! ''
shout Billy Mink .
A grin crept over the sharp little old face peer out from the bulrush .
`` Hi , yo ` self ! ''
he shout , for it really be Unc ' Billy Possum .
`` What be you do over here ? ''
call Little Joe Otter .
`` Just a-looking round , '' reply Unc ' Billy Possum , his eye twinkle .
`` Have you hear about Reddy Fox ? ''
shout Billy Mink .
`` Ah do jes ' come from his home , '' reply Unc ' Billy Possum .
`` How be he ? ''
ask Little Joe Otter .
`` Po ` ly , he sho ` ly be po ` ly , '' reply Unc ' Billy Possum , shake his head soberly .
Then Unc ' Billy tell Billy Mink and Little Joe Otter how Reddy Fox be so stiff and sore and sick that he could n't get anything to eat for himself , and how old Granny Fox have lose a chicken which she have catch for him .
`` Serves him right ! ''
exclaim Billy Mink , who have never forget how Reddy Fox fool him and catch the most fish once upon a time .
Unc ' Billy nod his head .
`` Yo ' be right .
Yo ' cert ` nly be right .
Yes , Suh , Ah reckons yo ' be right .
Was yo ' ever hungry , Billy Mink -- real hungry ? ''
ask Unc ' Billy Possum .
Billy Mink thought of the time when he go without his dinner because Mr. Night Heron have gobble it up , when Billy have leave it in a temper .
He nod his head .
`` Ah be just a-wondering , '' continue Une ' Billy Possum , `` how it would seem to be right smart powerful hungry and not be able to hunt fo ' anything to eat . ''
For a few minute no one say a word .
Then Billy Mink stand up and stretch .
`` Good-by , '' say Billy Mink .
`` Where be you go so suddenly ? ''
demand Little Joe Otter .
`` I 'm go to catch a fish and take it up to Reddy Fox , if you must know ! ''
snap Billy Mink .
`` Good ! ''
cry Little Joe Otter .
`` You need n't think that you can have all the fun to yourself either , Billy Mink .
I 'm go with you . ''
There be a splash in the Smiling Pool , and Unc ' Billy Possum be leave look out on nothing but the Smiling Pool and the Big Rock .
He smile to himself a he turn away .
`` Ah reckon Ah 'll sho ' have to do my share , too , '' say he .
And so it happen that when old Granny Fox finally reach home with nothing but a little wood mouse for Reddy , she find him take a nap , his stomach as full a it could be .
And just a little way off be two fish tail and the feather of a little duck .
XVII .
Farmer Brown 's Boy Is Determined Farmer Brown 's boy have make up his mind .
When he shut his teeth with a click and draw his lip together into a thin , straight line , those who know him be sure that Farmer Brown 's boy have make up his mind .
That be just what he have do now .
He be clean his gun , and a he work he be think of his pet chicken and of all the other chicken that Reddy Fox have take .
`` I 'm go to get that fox if it take all summer ! ''
exclaim Farmer Brown 's boy .
`` I ought to have get him the other day when I have a shot at him .
Next time well , we 'll see , Mr. Fox , what will happen next time . ''
Now someone hear Farmer Brown 's boy , heard everything he say , though Farmer Brown 's boy do n't know it .
It be Unc ' Billy Possum , who be hide in the very pile of wood on which Farmer Brown 's boy be sit .
Unc ' Billy prick up his ear .
He do n't like the tone of voice in which Farmer Brown 's boy spoke .
He think of Reddy Fox still so stiff and sore and lame that he could hardly walk , all from the shot which Farmer Brown 's boy thought have miss .
`` There be n't gwine to be any next time .
No , Suh , there be n't gwine to be any next time .
Ah sho ` ly doan love Reddy Fox , but Ah ca n't nohow let him be shoot again .
Ah cert ` nly ca n't ! ''
mutter Unc ' Billy Possum to himself .
Of course , Farmer Brown 's boy do n't hear him .
He do n't hear him and he do n't see him when Unc ' Billy Possum creep out of the back side of the woodpile and scurry under the henhouse .
He be too intent on his plan to catch Reddy Fox .
`` I 'm just go to hunt over the Green Meadows and through the Green Forest until I get that fox ! ''
say Farmer Brown 's boy , and a he say it he look very fierce , a if he really mean it .
`` I 'm not go to have my chicken steal any more !
No , Sir-e-e !
That fox have get a home somewhere on the Green Meadows or in the Green Forest , and I 'm go to find it .
Then watch out , Mr. Fox ! ''
Farmer Brown 's boy whistle for Bowser the Hound and start for the Green Forest .
Unc ' Billy Possum poke his sharp little old face out from under the henhouse and watch them go .
Usually Unc ' Billy be grin , but now there be n't any grin , not the least sign of one .
Instead Unc ' Billy Possum look worried .
`` There go that boy with a gun , and nobody know what 'll happen when it go off .
If he ca n't find Reddy Fox , just as likely a not he 'll point it at somebody else just fo ' fun .
Ah hope he doan meet up with mah ol ' woman or any of mah li'l ' pickaninny .
Ah 'm plumb afraid of a boy with a gun , Ah be .
` Pears like he doan have any sense .
Ah reckon Ah well be move along right smart and tell mah family to stay right close in the ol ' hollow tree , '' mutter Unc ' Billy Possum , slip out from his hide place .
Then Unc ' Billy begin to run as fast a he could toward the Green Forest .
XVIII .
The Hunt for Reddy Fox `` Trouble , trouble , trouble , I feel it in the air ; Trouble , trouble , trouble , it 's round me everywhere . ''
Old Granny Fox mutter this over and over , a she keep walk around uneasily and sniff the air .
`` I do n't see any trouble and I do n't feel any trouble in the air .
It 's all in the sore place where I be shoot , '' say Reddy Fox , who be stretch out on the doorstep of their home .
`` That 's because you have n't get any sense .
When you do get some and learn to look where you be go , you wo n't get shot from behind old tree trunk and you will be able to feel trouble when it be near , without wait for it to show itself .
Now I feel trouble .
You go down into the house and stay there ! ''
Granny Fox stop to test the air with her nose , just a she have be test it for the last ten minute .
`` I do n't want to go in , '' whine Reddy Fox .
`` It 's nice and warm out here , and I feel a lot good than when I be curl up way down there in the dark . ''
Old Granny Fox turn , and her eye blaze a she look at Reddy Fox .
She do n't say a word .
She do n't have to .
Reddy just crawl into his house , mutter to himself .
Granny stick her head in at the door .
`` Do n't you come out until I come back , '' she order .
Then she add : `` Farmer Brown 's boy be come with his gun . ''
Reddy Fox shiver when he hear that .
He do n't believe Granny Fox .
He think she be say that just to scare him and make him stay inside .
But he shiver just the same .
You see , he know now what it mean to be shoot , for he be still too stiff and sore to run , all because he have go too near Farmer Brown 's boy and his gun .
But old Granny Fox have not be fool when she tell Reddy Fox that Farmer Brown 's boy be come with a gun .
It be true .
He be come down the Lone Little Path , and ahead of him be trot Bowser the Hound .
How do old Granny Fox know it ?
She just felt it !
She do n't hear them , she do n't see them , and she do n't smell them ; she just felt that they be come .
So as soon a she saw that Reddy Fox have obey her , she be off like a little red flash .
`` It wo n't do to let them find our home , '' say Granny to herself , a she disappear in the Green Forest .
First she hurry to a little point on the hill where she could look down the Lone Little Path .
Just a she expect , she saw Farmer Brown 's boy , and ahead of him , sniff at every bush and all along the Lone Little Path , be Bowser the Hound .
Old Granny Fox wait to see no more .
She run as fast a she could in a big circle which bring her out on the Lone Little Path below Farmer Brown 's boy and Bowser the Hound , but where they could n't see her , because of a turn in the Lone Little Path .
She trot down the Lone Little Path a very little way and then turn into the wood and hurry back up the hill , where she sit down and wait .
In a few minute she hear Bowser 's great voice .
He have smell her track in the Lone Little Path and be follow it .
Old Granny Fox grin .
You see , she be plan to lead them far , far away from the home where Reddy Fox be hide , for it would not do to have them find it .
And Farmer Brown 's boy also grin , a he hear the voice of Bowser the Hound .
`` I 'll hunt that fox until I get him , '' he say .
You see , he do n't know anything about old Granny Fox ; he think Bowser be follow Reddy Fox .
XIX Unc ' Billy Possum Gives Warning `` What 's the matter with you , Unc ' Billy ?
You look a if you have lose your last friend . ''
It be Jimmy Skunk who speak .
Unc ' Billy Possum stop short .
He have be hurry so fast that he have n't see Jimmy Skunk at all .
`` Matter enuff , Suh !
Matter enuff ! ''
say Unc ' Billy Possum , when he could get his breath .
`` Do you hear that noise ? ''
`` Sure , I hear that noise .
That 's only Bowser the Hound chase old Granny Fox .
When she get tired she 'll lose him , '' reply Jimmy Skunk .
`` What be you worry about Bowser the Hound for ? ''
`` Bowser the Hound will have to be smart than he be now befo ' he can worry me , Ah reckon , '' say Unc ' Billy Possum scornfully .
`` It be n't Bowser the Hound ; it 's Farmer Brown 's boy and his gun ! ''
Then Unc ' Billy tell Jimmy Skunk how he have be hide in the woodpile at Farmer Brown 's and have hear Farmer Brown 's boy say that he be go to hunt over the Green Meadows and through the Green Forest until he get Reddy Fox .
`` What of it ? ''
ask Jimmy Skunk .
`` If he get Reddy Fox , so much the good .
Reddy always do make trouble for other people .
I do n't see what you 're worry about Reddy Fox for .
He 's big enough to take care of himself . ''
`` Yo ' cert ` nly be plumb slow in your wit this morning , Jimmy Skunk , yo ' cert ` nly be plumb slow !
Supposing yo ' should meet up with Farmer Brown 's boy with that gun in his hand and suppose he have grow tire of watch fo ' Reddy Fox .
That gun might go off , Jimmy Skunk ; it might go off when it be point right straight at yo ' ! ''
say Unc ' Billy Possum .
Jimmy Skunk look serious .
`` That 's so , Unc ' Billy , that 's so ! ''
he say .
`` Boys with gun do get dreadfully careless , dreadfully careless .
They do n't seem to think anything about the feeling of those likely to get hurt when the gun go off .
What be you thinking of do , Unc ' Billy ? ''
`` Just pass the word along so everybody in the Green Meadows and in the Green Forest will keep out of the way of Farmer Brown 's boy , '' reply Unc ' Billy Possum .
`` Good idea , Unc ' Billy !
I 'll help you , '' say Jimmy Skunk .
So Unc ' Billy Possum go one way , and Jimmy Skunk go another way .
And everyone they tell hurry to tell someone else .
Happy Jack Squirrel tell Chatterer the Red Squirrel ; Chatterer tell Striped Chipmunk , and Striped Chipmunk tell Danny Meadow Mouse .
Danny Meadow Mouse tell Johnny Chuck ; Johnny Chuck tell Peter Rabbit ; Peter Rabbit tell Jumper the Hare ; Jumper the Hare tell Prickly Porky ; Prickly Porky tell Bobby Coon ; Bobby Coon tell Billy Mink ; Billy Mink tell Little Joe Otter ; Little Joe Otter tell Jerry Muskrat , and Jerry Muskrat tell Grandfather Frog .
And everybody hasten to hide from Farmer Brown 's boy and his terrible gun .
By and by Farmer Brown 's boy notice how still it be in the Green Forest .
Nowhere do he see or hear a bird .
Nowhere could he catch a glimpse of anybody who wear fur .
`` That fox must have scar away all the other animal and drive away all the bird .
I 'll get him !
See if I do n't ! ''
mutter Farmer Brown 's boy , and never once guess that they be hide from him .
XX .
Old Granny Fox Makes a Mistake Old Granny Fox be run through the overgrown old pasture , way up back of Farmer Brown 's .
She be cross and tired and hot , for it be a very warm day .
Behind her come Bowser the Hound , his nose in Granny 's track , and make a great noise with his big voice .
Granny Fox be cross because she be tire .
She have n't do much running lately .
She do n't mind run when the weather be cold , but now -- `` Oh dear , it be hot ! ''
sigh old Granny Fox , a she stop a minute to rest .
Now old Granny Fox be very , very smart and very , very wise .
She know all the trick with which foxes fool those who try to catch them .
She know that she could fool Bowser the Hound and puzzle him so that he would n't be able to follow her track at all .
But she be n't ready to do that yet .
No , indeed !
Old Granny Fox be take great care to see that her track be easy to follow .
She want Bowser the Hound to follow them , although it make her tired and hot and cross .
Why do she ?
Well , you see , she be try to lead him , and with him Farmer Brown 's boy , far , far away from the home where Reddy Fox be nurse the wound that he have receive when Farmer Brown 's boy have shoot at him a few day before .
`` Bow , wow , wow ! ''
roar Bowser the Hound , follow every twist and turn which Granny Fox make , just a she want him to .
Back and forth across the old pasture and way up among the rock on the edge of the mountain Granny Fox lead Bowser the Hound .
It be a long , long , long way from the Green Meadows and the Green Forest .
Granny Fox have make it a long way purposely .
She be willing to be tire herself if she could also tire Bowser the Hound and Farmer Brown 's boy .
She want to tire them so that when she finally puzzle and fool them and leave them there , they would be too tired to go back to the Green Meadows .
By and by Granny Fox come to a hole in the ground , an old house that have once belong to her grandfather .
Now this old house have a back door hidden close beside the hollow trunk of a fall tree .
Old Granny Fox just run through the house , out the back door , through the hollow tree , and then jump into a little brook where there be hardly more than enough water to wet her foot .
Walking in the water , she leave no scent in her track .
Bowser the Hound come roar up to the front door of the old house .
Granny 's track lead right inside , and Bowser grow so excited that he make a tremendous noise .
At last he have find where Granny Fox live ; at least he think he have .
He be sure that she be inside , for there be her fresh track go inside and none come out .
Bowser the Hound never once think of look for a back door .
If he have , he would n't have be any the wiser , because , you know , old Granny Fox have slip away through the hollow tree trunk .
Granny Fox grin a she listen to the terrible fuss Bowser be make .
Then , when she have rest a little , she steal up on the hill where she could look down and see the entrance to the old deserted house .
She watch Bowser digging and barking .
After a while a worried look creep into the face of old Granny Fox .
`` Where 's Farmer Brown 's boy ?
I think surely he would follow Bowser the Hound , '' she mutter .
XXI .
Reddy Fox Disobeys When old Granny Fox have send Reddy Fox into the house and tell him to stay there until she return home , he have not want to mind , but he know that Granny Fox meant just what she say , and so he have crawl slowly down the long hall to the bedroom , way underground .
Pretty soon Reddy Fox hear a voice .
It be very faint , for you know Reddy be in his bedroom way underground , but he know it .
He prick up his ear and listen .
It be the voice of Bowser the Hound , and Reddy know by the sound that Bowser be chase Granny Fox .
Reddy grin .
He be n't at all worried about Granny Fox , not the least little bit .
He know how smart she be and that whenever she want to , she could get rid of Bowser the Hound .
Then a sudden thought pop into Reddy 's head , and he grow sober .
`` Granny do feel trouble come , just a she say , '' he think .
Then Reddy Fox curl himself up and try to sleep .
He intend to mind and not put his little black nose outside until old Granny Fox return .
But somehow Reddy could n't get to sleep .
His bedroom be small , and he be so stiff and sore that he could not get comfortable .
He twist and turn and fidget .
The more he fidget , the more uncomfortable he grow .
He think of the warm sunshine outside and how comfortable he would be , stretch out full length on the doorstep .
It would take the soreness out of his leg .
Something must have happen to Granny to keep her so long .
If she have know that she be go to be go such a long time , she would n't have tell him to stay until she come back , think Reddy .
By and by Reddy Fox creep a little way up the long , dark hall .
He could just see the sunlight on the doorstep .
Pretty soon he go a little bit nearer .
He be n't go to disobey old Granny Fox .
Oh , no !
No , indeed !
She have tell him to stay in the house until she return .
She have n't say that he could n't look out !
Reddy crawl a little nearer to the open door and the sunlight .
`` Granny Fox be get old and timid .
Just a if my eye be n't as sharp a hers !
I 'd like to see Farmer Brown 's boy get near me when I be really on the watch , '' say Reddy Fox to himself .
And then he creep a little nearer to the open door .
How bright and warm and pleasant it do look outside !
Reddy just know that he would feel ever and ever so much good if he could stretch out on the doorstep .
He could hear Jenny Wren fussing and scolding at someone or something , and he wonder what it could be .
He creep just a wee bit nearer .
He could hear Bowser 's voice , but it be so faint that he have to prick up his sharp little ear and listen with all his might to hear it at all .
`` Granny 's lead them way off on the mountain .
Good old Granny ! ''
think Reddy Fox .
Then he crawl right up to the very doorway .
He could still hear Jenny Wren scolding and fussing .
`` What do ail her ?
`` If it 's hot or if it 's cold , Jenny Wren will always scold .
From morn till night the whole day long Her limber tongue be go strong .
`` I 'm go to find out what it mean , '' say Reddy , talk to himself .
Reddy Fox poke his head out and -- look straight into the freckled face of Farmer Brown 's boy and the muzzle of that dreadful gun !
XXII .
Ol ' Mistah Buzzard 's Keen Sight Old Granny Fox have think that when she fool Bowser the Hound up in the old pasture on the edge of the mountain she could take her time go home .
She be tire and hot , and she have plan to pick out the shady path go back .
She have think that Farmer Brown 's boy would soon join Bowser the Hound , when Bowser make such a fuss about have find the old house into which Granny Fox have run .
But Farmer Brown 's boy have not yet appear , and Granny Fox be get worried .
Could it be that he have not follow Bowser the Hound , after all ?
Granny Fox go out on a high point and look , but she could see nothing of Farmer Brown 's boy and his gun .
Just then Ol ' Mistah Buzzard come sail down out of the blue , blue sky and settle himself on a tall , dead tree .
Now Granny Fox have n't forget how Ol ' Mistah Buzzard have warn Peter Rabbit just a she be about to pounce on him , but she suddenly think that Ol ' Mistah Buzzard might be of use to her .
So old Granny Fox smooth out her skirt and walk over to the foot of the tree where Ol ' Mistah Buzzard sit .
`` How do you do today , neighbor Buzzard ? ''
inquired Granny Fox , smile up at Ol ' Mistah Buzzard .
`` Ah 'm so a to be up and about , thank yo ' , '' reply Ol ' Mistah Buzzard , spread his wing out so that air could blow under them .
`` My ! ''
exclaim old Granny Fox , `` what splendid great wing you have , Mistah Buzzard !
It must be grand to be able to fly .
I suppose you can see a great deal from way up there in the blue , blue sky , Mistah Buzzard . ''
Ol ' Mistah Buzzard felt flatter .
`` Yes , '' say he , `` Ah can see all that 's go on on the Green Meadows and in the Green Forest . ''
`` Oh , Mistah Buzzard , you do n't really mean that ! ''
exclaim old Granny Fox , just a if she want to believe it , but could n't .
`` Yes , Ah can ! ''
reply Ol ' Mistah Buzzard .
`` Really , Mistah Buzzard ?
Really ?
Oh , I ca n't believe that your eye be so sharp a all that !
Now I know where Bowser the Hound be and where Farmer Brown 's boy be , but I do n't believe you can see them , '' say Granny Fox .
Ol ' Mistah Buzzard never say a word but spread his broad wing and in a few minute he have sail up , up , up until he look like just a tiny speck to old Granny Fox .
Now old Granny Fox have not tell the truth when she say she know where Farmer Brown 's boy be .
She think she would trick Ol ' Mistah Buzzard into tell her .
In a few minute down come Ol ' Mistah Buzzard .
`` Bowser the Hound be up in the old back pasture , '' say he .
`` Right ! ''
cry old Granny Fox , clap her hand .
`` And where be Farmer Brown 's boy ? ''
`` Farmer Brown 's boy be ... '' Ol ' Mistah Buzzard pause .
`` Where ?
Where ? ''
ask Granny Fox , so eagerly that Ol ' Mistah Buzzard look at her sharply .
`` Yo ' say you know , so what 's the use of tell yo ' ? ''
say Ol ' Mistah Buzzard .
Then he add : `` But if Ah be yo ' , Ah cert ` nly would get home right smart soon . ''
`` Why ?
Do , do tell me what you saw , Mistah Buzzard ! ''
beg Granny Fox .
But Ol ' Mistah Buzzard would n't say another word , so old Granny Fox start for home as fast a she could run .
`` Oh dear , I do hope Reddy Fox mind me and stay in the house , '' she mutter .
XXII Granny Fox Has a Terrible Scare Old Granny Fox felt her heart sink way down to her toe , for she felt sure Ol ' Mistah Buzzard have see Farmer Brown 's boy and his gun over near the house where Reddy Fox be nurse his wound , or he would n't have advise her to hurry home .
She be already very tired and hot from the long run to lead Bowser the Hound away from the Green Meadows .
She have think to walk home along shady path and cool off , but now she must run faster than ever , for she must know if Farmer Brown 's boy have find her house .
`` It 's lucky I tell Reddy Fox to go inside and not come out till I return ; it 's very lucky I do that , '' think Granny Fox a she run .
Presently she hear voice sing .
They seem to be in the treetop over her head .
`` Happily we dance and play All the livelong sunny day !
Happily we run and race And win or lose with smile face ! ''
Granny Fox know the voice , and she look up .
Just a she expect , she saw the Merry Little Breezes of Old Mother West Wind play among the leaf .
Just then one of them look down and saw her .
`` There 's old Granny Fox !
Just see how hot and tired she look .
Let 's go down and cool her off ! ''
shout the Merry Little Breeze .
In a flash they be all down out of the treetop and dance around old Granny Fox , cool her off .
Of course , Granny Fox keep right on run .
She be too worried not to .
But the Merry Little Breezes keep right beside her , and it be not nearly as hard run now a it have be .
`` Have you see Farmer Brown 's boy ? ''
pant Granny Fox .
`` Oh , yes !
We saw him just a little while ago over near your house , Granny Fox .
We pull his hat off , just to hear him scold , '' shout the Merry Little Breezes , and then they tickle and laugh a if they have have a good time with Farmer Brown 's boy .
But old Granny Fox do n't laugh -- oh , my , no , indeed !
Her heart go low still , and she do her best to run faster .
Pretty soon she come out on the top of the hill where she could look , and then it seem a if her heart come right up in her mouth and stop beating .
Her eye pop almost out of her head .
There be Farmer Brown 's boy stand right in front of the door of her home .
And while she be watch , what should Reddy Fox do but stick his head out the door .
Old Granny Fox saw the gun of Farmer Brown 's boy point right at Reddy and she clap both hand over her eye to shut out the dreadful sight .
Then she wait for the bang of the gun .
It do n't come .
Then Granny peep through her finger .
Farmer Brown 's boy be still there , but Reddy Fox have disappear inside the house .
Granny Fox sigh in relief .
It have be a terrible scare , the bad she could remember .
XXIV .
Granny and Reddy Have To Move `` I do n't want to move , '' whine Reddy Fox .
`` I 'm too sore to walk . ''
Old Granny Fox give him a shove .
`` You go along and do a I say ! ''
she snap .
`` If you have mind me , we would n't have to move .
It 's all your own fault .
The wonder be that you be n't kill when you poke your head out right in front of Farmer Brown 's boy .
Now that he know where we live , he will give u no peace .
Move along lively now !
This be the best home I have ever have , and now I 've get to leave it .
Oh dear !
Oh dear ! ''
Reddy Fox hobble along up the long hall and out the front door .
He be walk on three leg , and at every step he make a face because , you know , it hurt so to walk .
The little star , look down from the sky , saw Reddy Fox limp out the door of the house he have live in so long , and right behind him come old Granny Fox .
Granny sigh and wipe away a tear , a she say good-by to her old home .
Reddy Fox be think too much of his own trouble to notice how badly Granny Fox be feel .
Every few step he have to sit down and rest because it hurt him so to walk .
`` I do n't see the use of move tonight , anyway .
It would be a lot easy and pleasanter when the sun be shin .
This night air make me so stiff that I know I never will get over it , '' grumble Reddy Fox .
Old Granny Fox listen to him for a while , and then she lose patience .
Yes , Sir , Granny Fox lose patience .
She box Reddy Fox first on one ear and then on the other .
Reddy begin to snivel .
`` Stop that ! ''
say Granny Fox sharply .
`` Do you want all the neighbor to know that we have get to move ?
They 'll find it out soon enough .
Now come along without any more fuss .
If you do n't , I 'll just go off and leave you to shift for yourself .
